Looking extremely arrogant, he loudly said, “The Qing and Niu combo is back in Revered Ancient! Hello, ladies and gentlemen!”

The familiar voice struck the imperial capital of humankind like a bolt of lightning from ancient times! All of the human cultivators were instantly shaken to the core.

Ningyan had been standing on a beacon tower, wracked with anxiety and pessimism. For Revered Ancient to face catastrophe and then have a host of unknown cultivators show up had filled him with profound unease. But as soon as he heard those words, he looked up, his face and eyes full of a level of unprecedented shock that surpassed anything he had ever experienced in his life.

Staring up at that blurry figure with a look of blank incredulity, he blurted, “Captain!”

A buzz began to build among the humans in the imperial capital. Countless cultivators stood there, stunned, their minds reeling. Every person who had ever come to know Erniu felt immeasurable shock, and looked utterly taken aback.

Only a moment before, they had been facing catastrophe, and had felt incredibly nervous. Erniu’s arrival on the scene was just too unexpected. And they simply couldn’t understand how Erniu could be connected to the eleven Grand Emperors. They just didn’t know how to react.

Erniu hovered above, looking incredibly pleased with himself. This was exactly why he had rushed to jump out first. Eyebrows dancing up and down, he cleared his throat, clasped his hands behind his back, and opened his mouth to launch into a speech.

But then, Zhou Zhengli, looking incomparably solemn, flew forward, clasped his hands together, and bowed deeply.

“Zhou Zhengli offers respectful greetings, Your Majesty!”

He spoke loudly and with great force, his eyes shining brightly as if he were the most sincere believer imaginable.

As his voice drifted out, Li Mengtu flew forward and offered a similarly deep bow. Looking very serious, he said, “Li Mengtu offers respectful greetings, Your Majesty!”

Sir Vilespirit didn’t want to fall behind the others. Wiping the wicked expression off his face, which made him look a lot more normal, he stepped forward, his eyes burning as if with fire, and his cultivation base surging. As a result, fluctuations swept out from him, carrying his voice even further as he said, “Sir Vilespirit offers respectful greetings, Your Majesty!”

Yuanshan Su calmly bowed her head. Then came Sir Star Ring. He was still as proud as ever. But after everything he had experienced in his journeys with Xu Qing, the arrogant look on his face actually didn’t match his feelings inside. In reality, he deeply approved of Xu Qing. Therefore... thinking back to what Xu Qing had done back in his own home, the Fifth Star Ring, he took a deep breath and bowed.

“Sir Star Ring offers... respectful greetings, Your Majesty.”

The words uttered by the Grand Emperors sent shock into the hearts of all the people. And it wasn’t just them. Daoist Bloodcloud and the other chosen who had left to deal with the holy lands Quasi-Immortals also bowed respectfully wherever they were. Their voices echoed out as well.

“We offer respectful greetings, Your Majesty!”

In another direction, Hordeslayer and Rampart, the immortal swords, were trembling. The voices that echoed out from the two brothers seemed filled with an excitement they had prepared long in advance.

“Your Majesty shakes the ancient and illuminates the present! You are the number one in the kosmos! Your immortal bearing and bones of jade surpass all that is mortal! Your daoist magics and divine abilities shock the soul of the world!”

“Your Majesty can dominate all heaven and earth! You are invincible in the world! Your pupils are stars that contain the cosmos, and the tip of your sword can pierce the highest clouds in the dome of heaven!”

To add to the effect, they sent immortal light streaming out of the immortal sword forms, which became a five-colored halo that spread in all directions.

Revered Ancient was shaken to the core! It had been shocking enough for these eleven Grand Emperors to suddenly show up. But the way they were bowing and offering respectful greetings was simply mind-blowing. All of the people of Revered Ancient and all of the holy lands cultivators reeled as they used their various methods of looking at the person these Grand Emperors were showing respect to.

An instant later, a figure strode out behind Erniu. As he approached, his features became increasingly clear. And when everyone could see him....

Heaven and earth seemed filled with radiant brightness. All cultivators who saw him were astonished. This person’s aura could overthrow anything from before. The gods who sensed it were stupefied.

Some people recognized Erniu, others did not. But... the person who walked out behind Erniu and was offered respect by the Grand Emperors could shake heaven and earth. There was not one individual who didn’t know him! It was as if the arrival of Erniu, and the attention he attracted, was nothing but a foil for the person who came out after him.

Empress Summer Departure was a god, but at the moment, shē couldn’t suppress the shock within hēr, to the point where an expression of utter disbelief covered hēr face.

“Xu Qing!” she blurted.

The buzz got louder.

Up in the sky, Master Seventh smiled.

On the beacon tower in the imperial capital, Ningyan stared blankly. He was trembling. Erniu’s arrival had been a shock, but seeing the person behind him left Ningyan’s mind empty. “Th-that... that....”

The members of the nobility in the imperial capital looked on with disbelieving eyes.

The reactions in Sea-Sealing County were similar. Marquis Yao had pooled the various powers in Sea-Sealing County to create a huge mirror that showed what was happening in the capital. And when Marquis Yao saw who stepped out, his jaw dropped. Standing next to him was his sister, Yao Yunhui, who was equally stunned.

All of Xu Qing’s old friends, such as Kong Xianglong, struggled to breathe steadily. Wu Jianwu was there in the crowd, his mouth open as if to speak. And yet, at the moment, not one word of poetry would come out of his mouth. Also present were Zhang San, Ding Xue, Zhao Zhongheng, and all of the other people he knew in Sea-Sealing County. All were flabbergasted. They felt like they were in an illusion.

“Is that...?”

“He looks so familiar....”

“Th-that... that....”

Underneath Sea-Sealing County in the phoenix palace, a sharp exhalation broke the silence. At the same time, an iron skewer flew out and took the form of Patriarch Golden Vajra Warrior, who gasped and rubbed his eyes.

Of course, there was Seven Blood Eyes and also... there was the Moonrite Region! The Heir Apparent and his siblings were visibly stunned. Ling’er’s eyes were shining.

“Big Bro Xu Qing....”

All of the species in Revered Ancient reacted similarly, including the gods. Sunfire, Moonfire, and numerous other gods worshiped by various species, and even hidden gods unknown to anyone, were all trembling.

Divine will and physical gazes gathered from all directions, converging on the person who was still in the middle of walking out into the open. Every step he took seemed to carry immense weight, shattering the air and prompting heavenly daos to offer allegiance to him.

He was like an emperor on patrol! He walked with an invincible momentum that came from having experienced countless hardships. As he passed, spirit energy and mutagen alike seemed to offer obeisance, and cleared the way for him.

As he appeared, his hair cascaded down like violet ink, giving him an unmatchable grace. A few strands of hair crossed his face, creating a slightly messy but incredibly enticing image. He was like the most prominent figure in all heaven and earth, someone that nobody could look away from.

His eyes were like deep, cool abysses of water, incredibly cold, but also full of infinite heavenly bodies that few people would dare to look into. Every time he blinked, those eyes glittered with incredibly sharp light. It was something that could pierce into the hearts of all people, so that wherever he looked, people were urged to bow their heads in respect.

It seemed as if he could seize control of the fates of all things in existence, all by exercising a mere thought. A wild wind swept around him, causing his black robe to sway with undeniable mightiness.

The material of the black robe was so luxurious that it seemed to bend darkness and light, as if it brimmed with mysterious power. It was as if the night itself was willing to be foil to him, and place all mysteries and profundities in contrast to his transcendent nature. Everything about him, from his aura to his physical appearance, was perfect.

And then, as everyone looked on, he took a few steps out, only to stop and look right at the ancient immortal and Master Seventh. When he stopped moving, all living beings seemed to fade. Mountains and rivers lost their color, and time itself stopped. Everything went completely and utterly silent. It was as if his return made him the only heaven to actually exist! He controlled who lived and died, and none could defy him.

He was Xu Qing!

He did not look at any of the people present except for one. Master Seventh.

Bowing deeply, he softly said, “I’m back, Master. When I became your apprentice, the oath mentioned that you would keep me safe. But today, I’ve come back as your apprentice... to defend you, Master!”

He was back! And the words he spoke echoed out into heaven and earth, into the ears of all species, and to all corners of Revered Ancient. Countless emotions surged, and in all regions of the land, people from all species joined their voices together in exultation. They were voices of excitement, anticipation, and hope!

“It’s Xu Qing!”

“The eleven Grand Emperors were bowing to him!”

“If Grand Emperors addressed him as Your Majesty, then... what cultivation base does he have??”

“Could it be...?”

“Could it be...?”

“Summer Immortal!!!”

Master Seventh roared with laughter.

Xu Qing looked at the ancient immortal who had brought catastrophe to Revered Ancient. His expression was extremely serious and forbidding.

“Now, about you. I’ve been waiting to meet you for a long time.”

Xu Qing’s pupils narrowed to pinpricks as something like starlight shot out from them. Boundless spirit power surged, like a heavenly river that spread in all directions. It turned into a huge immortal body!

The Grand Emperors bowed, and all living beings gasped. The air shattered. All of Revered Ancient trembled, and crevices spread out in the land.

The sky instantly filled with dark clouds, lightning danced, and everything shook. Canon and statute became the new laws in Revered Ancient! Time. Space. All magics. Space-time. All daos. Parallelism. Unification... and they all led to ontology!

Things had built up to a crescendo! Heavenly gales battered everything left and right.

Meanwhile, Xu Qing hovered in midair, his expression cold, his gaze placid as he looked at the ancient immortal. Even as the words he had just spoken drifted out, he waved his right hand. That action sent ripples through Revered Ancient, causing the dome of heaven to tremble.

“Seal the space above earth!”

When Xu Qing spoke, his words were a command that could not be ignored, and contained his independent ontology! They became a sealing power that... separated heaven from earth! They made it impossible for things on the earth to fly up into the sky!

As a result, gods and cultivators alike, whether they were from Revered Ancient or the holy lands, instantly lost their ability to fly, and fell trembling to the ground. And that was because this power to separate heaven and earth came from a Summer Immortal! Therefore, anyone under the level of a Summer Immortal or a True God could not defy them!

In the shortest of moments, only three figures were left in the air above the imperial capital of humankind.

Xu Qing.

The ancient immortal.

And Master Seventh!

“Master, please hold the rear line for me!” he said respectfully.

Master Seventh smiled, and the gratitude in his eyes grew deeper. With a slight nod, he fell back and landed on the ground next to Empress Summer Departure.

The empress still looked somewhat dazed as shē stared up at Xu Qing. Incredulity grew stronger in hēr heart, until shē couldn’t hold back from turning to Master Seventh and asking, “His cultivation base...?”

Master Seventh didn’t respond immediately. He waved his hand and made a grasping gesture, and the air rippled as Erniu appeared. Master Seventh quickly grabbed him by the throat and dragged him forth.

“Hey, be gentle, ya old fogey! That hurts! Ouch!” Erniu was soon dangling in Master Seventh’s hand like a baby chicken. All he could do was wave his hands and legs, and yell a bit. Yet he didn’t forget to smile apologetically and plaster an ingratiating look onto his face.

“Master,” he wailed fawningly. “I missed you so much!”

Master Seventh looked at Erniu. “Talk. What’s Fourth Sib’s cultivation base now? And who are those people?”

Erniu’s eyebrows danced up and down. He knew exactly which ‘people’ his Master had just referred to, and he was already prepared to launch into some grandiose bragging.

Before he could, Master Seventh interrupted, “Talk normally.”

Scowling on the verge of tears, Erniu finally sighed. “They’re from the Fifth Star Ring, and they’re all the subordinates of little Junior Brother. You listen to me, Master. Little Junior Brother really rocked it in the Fifth Star Ring. If you went there, you wouldn’t even come close to being as important as him. As for his cultivation base... well, I actually just ran into him again recently. At that point he was a Grand Emperor, and also happened to be good friends with an Immortal Lord.... I get the feeling that guy wants to steal your apprentice!”

When Master Seventh heard the term Immortal Lord, he shivered inwardly, but managed to prevent it from showing on his face. Except that Erniu’s next words were even more shocking.

“That Immortal Lord friend of his gave little Junior Brother a few goddesses. Apparently, each one of those goddesses has a God Lord as a dad.”

Master Seventh struggled to control his breathing. Next to him, the empress’ eyes went wide.

“Well,” Erniu continued, “I couldn’t be outdone in that way, so I took little Ah Qing to the tomb of a God Paragon.... As it turned out, that God Paragon was still alive...” All of a sudden, Erniu realized that Master Seventh was gripping his throat a lot harder than before. “Aiyaaaa. That hurts! Agh! Gentler, please, Master!”

Master Seventh loosened his grip. He had taken the story about the Immortal Lord in stride, and even the mention of the God Lord. But then he heard ‘God Paragon.’ That was a level he had only speculated about, and he was aware that it was basically the most paramount level attainable in any given star ring! But apparently, his disaster of an apprentice had actually gone to the tomb of a God Paragon!

Taking a deep breath, Master Seventh growled, “Keep talking!”

Erniu blinked a few times. Inside, he was feeling very pleased with himself. The old fogey is definitely going to look at me in a new light now!

He cleared his throat. “I didn’t really do much in that tomb. I just accidentally devoured a God Lord. Supposedly he was a pretty ferocious God Lord, though. Anyway, Eminent Desolation showed up, and things got really dicey. So I quickly saved little Ah Qing and took him into a space-time vortex....

“Inside the vortex, we split up. Later on, I got worried about little Ah Qing, so I put everything on the line to find him. After I found him, little Ah Qing was crying and whatnot. I felt so bad. Being as soft-hearted as I am, I helped him reach immortal ascension. And that was when he stopped crying.”

Master Seventh frowned and was about to say something. However, that was when something really dramatic happened overhead!

Master Seventh, the empress, and Erniu alike all looked up. They weren’t the only ones. The powerful experts of countless species, regardless of where they were, used divine will to look at the imperial capital of humankind! Specifically, they focused on Xu Qing, and they focused on the battle that would determine what happened to Revered Ancient! freewebnovel.com

High in the canopy of heaven, surrounded by boundless radiant light... was the ancient immortal! The ancient immortal took a step forward, and ripples spread through the sky. Astonishing momentum caused Revered Ancient to tremble, ripping apart the dome of heaven to reveal the starry sky. The ancient immortal hovered underneath that starry sky, a sea of stars behind him, as if he were fused with that sky. And then his grim gaze landed on Xu Qing.

“A young Summer Immortal...” he said in a raspy voice. “Well, since you’ve been waiting for me, then... I’d like to see how strong you are, and whether or not your words live up to their implication!”

The ancient immortal, who looked like a corpse that had just climbed out of a grave, lifted his hand and pointed at Xu Qing!

That gesture caused his canon to build within him. Instantly, wild colors flashed and winds screamed. The sky shook, and the starry sky seemed to become more profound. Heaven-shaking, earth-shattering power surged from the ancient immortal, becoming an unstoppable momentum, stirring countless natural and magical laws, and ultimately turning into a blue drop of water!

That drop of water pulsed with a hair-raising mightiness, that caused anyone who sensed it to shake in body and soul. It felt like the mightiness might crush them out of existence, or rip them to shreds.

Even species who were a great distance away felt the same effects, and experienced a sense of impending catastrophe.

That drop of water came from a Summer Immortal, and contained immortal might! The moment it appeared, the ancient immortal flicked his finger, and the drop of water shot toward Xu Qing!

Even more terrifying to all of the living beings in Revered Ancient was that as the water drop neared Xu Qing, it multiplied! It started as one water drop, but became two. The two then became four. The four, eight. In the blink of an eye, one water drop turned into too many water drops to count. It was an astonishing blue sea! One drop had become a sea!

The sea swept forth, growing ever closer to Xu Qing. Where it passed, the air shattered, the sky was obfuscated, and the starry sky blessed it. As a result, the sea contained a will of space-time and the stipulations of parallelism! It was as if... it contained everything!

The outer layer was a tide of space-time. The sea seemed to come from an infinite number of worlds! This was the might of a Summer Immortal. Even though he did not cultivate the canon of space-time, after reaching a certain level, all daos become the same thing!

All living beings were stunned. And that was because, in their eyes, there was no sea!

The actions of Summer Immortals surpassed their perceptions. Not even the empress could see everything that was happening. It was all a blur. And thus, all onlookers, be they in the imperial capital or Revered Ancient as a whole, saw nothing but a host of abstract, complicated vortexes!

Only Master Seventh could clearly see the great sea, and his expression was incomparably serious.

And yet, despite all that, Xu Qing remained calm the entire time. He looked at the destructive sea of canon screaming toward him from the Summer Immortal, and he wasn’t surprised at all. Nor did he shrink back. Instead, he extended his right hand... and gently lowered it!

The tips of his fingers brushed the boundless sea waves! The moment they made contact, something completely unimaginable occurred in front of the eyes of the people of Revered Ancient! The numerous abstract vortexes began to crumble as if they were melting!

To Master Seventh’s astonishment, things changed in his view as well. When Xu Qing’s fingers touched the blue sea, Master Seventh clearly saw a huge rip appear in it. It was as if the elements making it up were being extracted! And that was exactly what was happening!

Xu Qing was doing the extracting! First he extracted space-time, then he extracted parallelism. And then the sea, having been stabilized, only existed in the surrounding world! It was cut off from the outside. And the so-called ‘countless’ wills were transformed. Having become countable instead of countless, they ceased multiplying!

Master Seventh gasped as he saw the previously magnificent blue sea affected by Xu Qing’s mere fingers. It lost all of its previous blessings! It transformed from a collective to individuals! The sea broke apart into different drops of water! The water drops that had been fused together were now split apart.

And then something happened that provoked a reaction from the ancient immortal. The changes to the sea continued. After becoming individual water drops, those water drops... also experience extraction!

No longer were they single water drops. They became... flat slips of water! And that was because Xu Qing had extracted their height! The water droplets completely lost any concept of height. They became just like the images he had seen in the second world in the Aurora Immortal Palace!

And yet, the transformations continued! The flat slips of water transformed again, becoming threads. Then they became singularities, after which they were completely and utterly wiped out.

None of them existed any longer.

All of this takes a bit of time to describe, but in the time it takes a spark to fly off a piece of flint, the entire sea became nothing.

No one other than Master Seventh understood what had just happened. Only he knew that, although it simply looked like a water drop had become a sea, the reality was that the presence of canon made the entire thing extremely deadly and dangerous. Not even he was confident that he could have dealt with that threat. And he knew that if Xu Qing hadn’t been able to deal with it, he would have become just one of the drops of water in that sea.

The more Master Seventh understood about what was happening, the more astonished he was. And that was because... he had no idea how Xu Qing had dealt with the canon in the sea!

The ancient immortal’s pupils constricted. He was now looking at Xu Qing as if he were an extremely dangerous enemy. “Your canon...?”

Xu Qing’s expression was the same as ever as he lifted his foot and took a step toward the ancient immortal. “If your canon has nothing but the concept of ‘countlessness,’ then... you might as well prepare to die!”

As the words left Xu Qing’s mouth, he took another step toward the ancient immortal, causing ripples to spread through the dome of heaven in concentric rings. Contained within them was a chaotic, primeval sensation.

That sensation was the hallmark of Fishing the Moon in the Well! Xu Qing had been using that divine ability for many years now. However, as his cultivation base climbed higher, it became increasingly ineffective. Using it against enemies under the level of an immortal was fine, but... it just wasn’t something that could be used on Summer Immortals.

However, this time, Xu Qing was unleashing it in a way that was different from before. In fact, in some ways, it was now substructurally different in a fundamental way! And that was because it contained... Xu Qing’s canon and statute!

On the way back to Revered Ancient, Xu Qing had taken some time to familiarize himself more deeply with his canon and statute, in some part due to encountering unexpected resistance. That was why he had arrived a bit late.

However, thanks to the fight with that unexpected enemy, he had suddenly gained a deeper understanding of his canon and statute. He knew that his canon was different from other Summer Immortals. After reaching a certain level, his canon... could produce statute!

Canon came first, statute came after. And statute... was something that only Immortal Lords could truly command.

“My canon and statute is that of ontology!”[1]

This so-called ontology was deeply profound and mysterious. Xu Qing’s enlightenment revealed to him that it was all-encompassing, and something that outsiders couldn’t possibly come to understand. Only the person commanding it could perceive the fundamental nature of the canon and statute.

Ontology is about disassembling complex structures and turning them into unique individualities.

Each step Xu Qing took caused more ripples to spread. All the while, his aura rose to heaven-shaking, earth-shattering heights as new understanding of his canon and statute swirled within him.

The number of those individualities is tied to the fundamental definition of ‘ontology.’ Unleashing it is about both disassembling and integration. It’s like taking one thing and disassembling it into many things.

That perception came from Xu Qing’s deep enlightenment. At the same time, it corroborated the direction of enlightenment he had pursued in the chaotic flow of space-time. After all, what he had called ‘unification’ was actually part of that process, as it took all of the independent parts and integrated them into a whole. It took countless things and unified them.

As a result of all the things he had done in the chaotic flow of space-time, he had taken that concept and used it to develop his canon and statute of ontology.

Take countless things and integrate them into one. Take one, and disassemble them into countless things. The process of disassembling and integration involves adjusting the components. It’s about increasing and decreasing them. And that is how ontology is made manifest!

And yet, as Xu Qing realized these things, he also came to the conclusion that he still didn’t realize the true nature of unification! Put precisely, the unification he was capable of now was likely a unification limited to a very specific scope.

If I consider the ‘one’ to be my dao, then my canon and statute will only be able to disassemble ‘one.’ But beyond that ‘one,’ there are even more ‘ones.’ It’s like how there are different godhoods among different gods, and different canons and statutes among cultivators. They... are all different ‘ones’ beyond my own dao of ‘one!’ To truly implement integration, and to become the actual ‘one and only,’ I need to reach a much higher level!!

A profound look appeared in Xu Qing’s eyes as he realized what direction he needed to pursue in the future.

If he succeeded, then the star ring would have no truly independent entities. It would be truly integrated, including all the canons and all the authorities. At that time, he would be the true ‘one and only,’ and would be the ultimate source of all.

Right now, there was no way for Xu Qing to truly grasp what that would mean, but he knew the direction to follow.

That must be my path to the level of Immortal Paragon! Right now, I have no way to be the ‘one and only.’ But... my canon and statute of ontology can adjust the disassembly and integration of all things, and upgrade them to an unimaginable level!

I can even change my divine abilities with that method! It’s the same for my magical techniques and all of my magical treasures! So at the moment....

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered. He had taken seven steps toward the ancient immortal, who looked like he was facing down the most deadly of enemies. At that point, Xu Qing stopped and waved his right hand.

Wild colors flashed in heaven and earth, all while deep rumbling sounds echoed out in all directions. Behind him, the void seemed to rip apart, and ripples spread from beneath his feet.

The dome of heaven seemed to turn into the surface of a well! Mighty waves kicked up, spreading through the sky, and turning the well into a heavenly sea. The water had reflections on it.

One reflection was of Xu Qing’s personal canon and statute of ontology! Another was the painter version of Xu Qing from that parallel spacetime, and of the final work he produced before he died! The painting in the divine ability caused the ripples on the well to calm down.

Next, Xu Qing exercised a thought, and his canon and statute became like ink which began to disassemble the divine ability. Fundamentally speaking, the divine ability known as Fishing the Moon in the Well was made of: space; an image of a moon; illusory reality; and conviction!

By using the canon and statute of ontology, all of that was being broken apart. The space was the world of a well, created out of nothing. The image of a moon was a reflection of the soul of an enemy, on the surface of the water. Illusory reality contained the transposition of what was real and what was false. It contained the power of rotation to turn the false into real, and to then fish out the true soul from the image of the moon. And then came conviction. The power of conviction turned into a huge hand which reached into the water and fished something out.

Before becoming a Summer Immortal and coming to understand the canon and statute of ontology, Xu Qing knew a bit about Fishing the Moon in the Well, but couldn’t truly explain the divine ability. But now, the true substructure of Fishing the Moon in the Well was clearly visible in Xu Qing’s heart and mind, and he could break it down into its components. And by making adjustments to it, he could upgrade the divine ability!

The very first thing he adjusted was the spatial power within it! He added to it! The previous spatial limitations instantly expanded. Instead of a well that contained heaven and earth, it was now a well that contained all parallels and all space-times. As a result, the personhood of the divine ability could encompass Summer Immortals!

And thus, Xu Qing’s ontology became like a well!

The moment the adjustment was complete, the sky in Revered Ancient blurred. It fused with the starry sky, and the ripples filling it overlapped, revealing a host of worlds. Terrifying mightiness weighed down, causing mountains to shake and rivers to flow backward. Fear filled the hearts of all living beings. Countless species were overwhelmed with amazement, and even gods were secretly moved.

Master Seventh inhaled sharply.

Even the ancient immortal was visibly taken aback. An intense sensation of deadly crisis hit him, which came from Xu Qing himself. And thus, he blurred into motion directly toward Xu Qing. His hope was to interrupt the divine ability before Xu Qing could bring that deadly crisis to fruition. All it took was a step to bring him very close to Xu Qing.

However, though it seemed like Xu Qing was slow in making the adjustments, the reality was that they occurred in the span of a single thought!

Even as the ancient immortal closed in, Fishing the Moon in the Well experienced the spatial bolstering, and the image of the moon was blessed by it!

It was instantly upgraded! It directly climbed to a higher level! Now it didn’t just create a reflection of the soul. The reflection included karma, fate, time, parallels, and all other traces of the target. This was... a reflection of omniscience!

Add in the blessing of conviction from Xu Qing’s immortal will and the power of parallelism to reverse illusion and reality, and the result was that Fishing the Moon in the Well truly was upgraded! In the blink of an eye, the divine ability Fishing the Moon in the Well changed dramatically!

Heaven and earth surged. The space-times of countless worlds, and also all parallels, became the surface of a well!

And it was all locked onto the ancient immortal threatening Xu Qing! Astonishingly, the soul of the ancient immortal was now visible in the water of the well! He was illuminated fully! What was more, all of his karma, fate, life trajectory, and everything else were revealed in the omniscience of the well water.

This was no longer just Fishing the Moon in the Well. This was a new divine ability that could eradicate immortals!

Xu Qing’s voice rang out into Revered Ancient, with a paramount will like the voice of heaven.

“Pluck stars from the vault of the universe!”

As he spoke, he reached out with his right hand. His immortal will thrummed, becoming a huge hand. Instead of entering the well... it reached toward all traces of the ancient immortal, as if it were about to pluck a star from the sky...

Then it fished out the immortal! The ancient immortal trembled as he sensed his karma being influenced, his fate being interfered with, his life force being affected, and his soul being peeled away. The sensation of deadly crisis grew more intense. He knew that an immortal magic which could pluck stars from the vault of the universe could encompass all aspects of himself. That included all versions of space-time and all parallels.

He couldn’t hide. But... instead of fighting back, he simply released his immortal will and allowed Xu Qing to fish it out. As the sensation of annihilation grew stronger, and as his karma, life force, and fate were fished out by Xu Qing, a critical momentum built. But the old man who looked like he had just crawled out of the grave actually looked at Xu Qing with glittering eyes.

“Before getting personally involved, I had no way to know what your canon is like.... But now that I’m immersed in your canon, I can tell that you’re truly a chosen. However....”

The ancient immortal looked at Xu Qing through the surface of water, and all of a sudden, a more intense aura of canon erupted from him.

“Back in the day, I was also a chosen! In the half of a sixty-year-cycle that’s passed, you might have matured, but I also gathered my thoughts from beyond. Furthermore, my canon... isn’t just that of countless concepts! You wanted to see, right? Then pay attention and see what my canon is really like!”

Immortal energy surged, causing the void to collapse, and influencing, not just Revered Ancient, but all of the areas and space-times affected by Xu Qing’s divine ability.

Beyond that, as the ancient immortal’s canon seethed, something completely outrageous happened to the reflection in the well! It was as if the reflection of his soul was an unbounded entity! Though Xu Qing had fished it out, the reality was that he had not!

It was the same with all of his karma. It was as if... his karma was unbounded! Similarly, all traces of his fate were also unbounded!

1. To reiterate the information from a few chapters ago, the Chinese character here can be interpreted many ways. The most common, in modern times, is ‘dimension,’ and later on, the author will even reference that ‘dimension’ meaning obliquely in certain wordplay and narrative elements. But the author’s explanation in this chapter makes it clear that he intends for this word to be more akin to the deep metaphorical/theological/cosmological definition of the word as it pertains to Chinese philosophy and belief systems. In terms of English, you can find information about ontology here. However, the meaning (both in Chinese and English), is devised by and explained by the author, and isn’t exactly what the dictionary definition is. ☜

Unbounded! Xu Qing thought.

Xu Qing hovered in the sky, peering into the well of myriad worlds, and the ancient immortal’s reflected fate, karma, and everything else. He had to admit that this ancient immortal definitely deserved to be called a chosen of his time. In fact, during all of his many battles in the Fifth Star Ring... he had never encountered someone with this kind of canon. It had reached a level beyond the control of ordinary Summer Immortals, and it was no exaggeration to say that it was very close to the level of an Immortal Lord.

He’s significantly stronger than when we met, half of a sixty-year-cycle ago!

Within the well, the ancient immortal looked up at Xu Qing. They were separated by the surface of the water, one being above it, the other below it. When their gazes met, the Revered Ancient mainland trembled. Mountains split open, the wind screamed, and increasingly intense pressure weighed down onto the hearts and minds of all living beings, turning into indescribable terror.

Meanwhile, the ancient immortal spoke in a raspy voice. “Countlessness is only the beginning of my canon. To complete the canon, I scatter countless streams of divine will to become countless clones. I even abandon my autonomy and allow a clone to become my main form. Then, I let the clones mature, devour each other, and fuse....

“The process caused the old me to dissipate. But my dao remains! Then, in the end, when my dao is complete, my canon is unbounded! I reconverged here, forming the power of statute. And now, the final leap requires only one thing. As for you... I can tell that you have not yet made the final leap.”

The ancient immortal’s profound eyes contained neither joy nor sadness. As he spoke, he lifted his right foot and then took a step forward. The moment he did, the surface of the well rumbled, and huge waves appeared.

It was like a massive tempest. Heaven and earth shook. The dome of the universe trembled. Everything was rocked.

The space within Xu Qing’s Fishing the Moon in the Well divine ability also vibrated. The true and false within, the illusory reality, distorted, and all the independent aspects of the divine ability showed signs of complete collapse. It didn’t seem like it could stand up to the force!

“I’ve seen canon like yours before,” the ancient immortal continued. “Ten thousand years ago in the Twenty-Seventh Star Ring, there was a god... who had something very similar to your canon. One thought to cover a myriad of worlds. Universal parallelism. Converge it into a flower of space-time, and wait for it to bear dao fruit.”[1]

As his voice drifted out, he took a second step. When that second footfall occurred, cracking sounds rang out from the surface of the well. Fissures appeared, snaking through the void, through space-time, and through parallelism.

The water of the well churned, becoming more turbid. What formed that turbidness... was the unbounded karma and unbounded fate of the ancient immortal! The true and false, the illusory reality, had reached their limit, and began to crumble.

The upgrade to the divine ability of Fishing the Moon in the Well was showing signs of irreversible collapse.

“In the end, you’re just too young and inexperienced.” Shaking his head, the ancient immortal took a third step. Heaven trembled and earth shuddered. The myriad worlds in the well collapsed. The true and false, the illusory and the reality, scattered further.

The world created by Fishing the Moon in the Well looked like a shattered mirror, and the fragments began to drift apart.

The image of the ancient immortal became complete once again beneath the shattered bits of the divine ability. But he looked very different. Though his face was still wrinkled and ancient, his eyes shone with unprecedented vitality! His long, flowing hair became flowing silver behind his back, like a galactic river pulsing with a unique aura. Outside of his body, seven-colored immortal mist swirled, the outworking of immortal might! His energy towered, provoking tideflows of heaven and earth, and dragging starlight down toward him. More than ever, he seemed like an unbounded entity.

A terrifying pressure erupted with mountain-toppling, sea-draining force, crushing everything in its path. The immortal prepared to take a fourth step.

“You talk too much,” Xu Qing said calmly. “Honestly, it’s annoying.”

As far as Xu Qing was concerned, his opponent did have a spectacular canon. That canon of the unbounded had put limitations on Xu Qing’s divine ability, to the point where it started to collapse, allowing the immortal to lunge out like a tiger released from a cage. But sometimes, the best way to deal with a tiger isn’t a strong cage! Sometimes, flexible ropes can work just as well!

Eyes glittering, Xu Qing lifted his right hand and then dropped it down. The shattered pieces of the divine ability began to transform.

Instantly, the countless fragments of the shattered divine ability became mirror shards. As they spun out in all directions, they reflected the karma and fate of the unbounded ancient immortal, revealing a host of scenes.

In every single mirror shard, it was possible to see traces of the ancient immortal! That was parallelism, in other words, different space-times and different worlds!

In those many worlds, the ancient immortal wasn’t always a cultivator! In some, he was mortal. In others, he was an animal. In other cases, he was a plant. He wasn’t always the same gender, either. Sometimes he was a man, sometimes he was a woman! Then....

Xu Qing suddenly rotated his hand. Eyes glinting coldly, he said, “Change!”

That one word caused the parallels to change. Myriad worlds were thrown into chaos! The mirror shards rippled and distorted as astonishing and unbelievable changes occurred.

The reflections of karma and fate in the shards were forcibly reversed and transformed. Men became women. Women became men. In some cases, cultivators became mortals. Humans became animals. Animals became plants. Everything changed.

And there was more. In the parallel worlds, natural disasters began to play out! Meteors fell and volcanoes erupted, evaporating seas! Rivers ran in reverse, devouring entire cities. In one mirror shard was an immortal tree that protected the entire world, which was a reflection of the karma of the ancient immortal. The tree started to wither from the roots, and the leaves fell like blood-red tears.

This was the power of Xu Qing’s canon and statute of ontology. In all of the parallels and space-times, he was making adjustments to the various independent versions.

The ancient immortal had been about to take a fourth step, but now he stopped in place. He saw his karma threads being devoured by that intangible power, and he saw his fate being infected. The previously smooth and glossy threads of fate were on the verge of being destroyed.

The silver light of immortals in his eyes started to dim, eventually turning into silver dust that drifted to the ground, leaving behind nothing but his turbid gaze. He struggled to circulate immortal power within him. However, the immortal might which he could usually manipulate with a mere thought seemed cut off from him by some vague barrier. The immortal light that formed on his fingertips became like dying moths that drifted to the ground below.

Ultimately, the depths of his soul were infected. Countless chaotic memory fragments assailed his sea of consciousness. The infected karma and fate brought a tempest with them. Everything rippled and distorted, like a painting dusted with poison powder. Even the color became poisonous, stabbing directly into his soul.

Veins bulged on his forehead, and his ears seemed to fill with millions upon millions of echoing curses. They were the wills of all those he had devoured in his life. Because of karmic infection, they had forgotten about their dao oaths, and only remembered the defiance they felt before being devoured.

And thus, the ancient immortal began to decline, turning from an immortal into a mortal. It looked as though even a slight push would cause him to disperse, and would result in the flame of his life force being wiped out.

And yet... Xu Qing didn’t advance. He just stood calmly in place observing.

Eventually, the ancient immortal shook his head. Speaking in a raspy voice, he said, “Quite an impressive toppling and transformation! Your infection succeeded. But you still face limitations. You’re not quite on my level....”

You... are still hiding your statute. I supposed you don’t want to use it casually. So the question is... are you going to use it now, or not?”

The ancient immortal said nothing at first. A moment later, he smiled. “Well I’m involved now. In reality... you’re waiting for something, aren’t you?”

Xu Qing shot a meaningful look back at the ancient immortal. “I’m waiting for the same thing as you. And time is on my side.”

The ancient immortal’s pupils constricted.

Xu Qing’s voice echoed out over the imperial capital of humankind, filling the sky and reaching the hearts and minds of powerful experts from countless species. Without exception, they were shaken to the core.

When Xu Qing saw that, his gaze hardened. Given the level of his cultivation base, he knew that this was no simplistic transformation. This was a true recovery! Actually, he didn’t resolve anything, nor did he recover. He molded a new version of himself!

It was creating something from nothing, or building without any foundation. It was taking the impossible and making it possible!

To a certain extent, a clash of statutes... came down to striking a blow to the most fundamental logic governing the opponent’s canon and statute, and using that to defeat them!

That internal danger often meant that victory and defeat could happen in the shortest of moments. Of course, the prerequisite... was to be able to understand the opponent’s statute!

There was an inexhaustible flow of mutagen that spread from the majestic river, going out in all directions to fill Revered Ancient. However, it lasted only an instant.

And that was because, high in the dome of heaven, the looming broken face of Eminent Desolation suddenly angled down slightly! The terrifying golden eyes in the godly river snapped shut without hesitation. Ninety-nine percent of the aura that had spread out was then retracted.

The mother river might be a God Paragon, but shē didn’t dare to show any more of hērself! Much less was shē willing to show up in hēr true form! In fact, shē didn’t even dare to send all of hēr divine will! This was only a scrap!

When the eyes closed in that tiny scrap of divine will, a figure appeared and was sent out of the drop of water! The figure was blue, and came with a terrifying pressure that erupted in all directions. Though the pressure was not the same as that of the golden eyes, it was still terrifying. However... it was not something that would attract the attention of the broken face like a God Paragon would.

The mother river had sent forth a God Lord! The moment hē appeared, hē summoned a massive fist that shot without hesitation... toward The Human World Sword!

The moment they made contact, rumbling sounds filled heaven and earth. The Human World Sword shook, and because of the mountain-toppling, sea-draining force of the fist, it had no choice but to give way.

The fist shivered, then shot forward explosively. It became a blue sea, filled with boundless force that shattered the air, split time, and aimed... at stopping Xu Qing. As the godly might in the form of a sea swept over Xu Qing, the God Lord no longer paid attention to The Human World Sword, nor did hē worry about fighting Xu Qing.

Shooting backward, hē grabbed the feeble ancient immortal and then flew up into the sky. Moving at top speed, hē quickly reached the highest point above. Hīs mission was to acquire the mother river’s pawn and escort him out! Hē really had no other intentions. Hē didn’t want to do anything else, or stay around for any longer than necessary. Though hē didn’t understand exactly why all of this was necessary, it was a mission from the mother river.

The pawn had failed, and had severed any connection to Revered Ancient. Therefore, the pawn held no further value. And yet, the mother river had taken a great risk by using a scrap of divine will to teleport hīm here. And hē absolutely had to take this specific cultivator back with hīm. Hē did not know why, but hē had to comply. Hē was not capable of resisting the will of the mother river, even though the very nature of this mission was absolutely terrifying to hīm.

Thankfully, the mother river permitted me to come as a clone that only contains one third of my true form.

With such thoughts in mind, hē swept up the ancient immortal and sped toward the sky. Along the way, hē looked at the broken face of Eminent Desolation. That one glance was enough to cause hīm to tremble in the depths of hīs god soul.

Moving at top speed, and drawing on the power of the mother river, hē broke free of Revered Ancient’s seal and entered the starry sky. Hē immediately raced away. Hē didn’t want to stay in the terrifying Revered Ancient for a moment longer. In fact, hē didn’t even want to be close to it.

Once I get far enough away from Revered Ancient, the mother river will pull me back....

All of this takes a bit of time to describe, but actually happened in the time it takes a spark to fly off a piece of flint.

The instant the God Lord sent by the mother river broke out into the starry sky, Xu Qing’s canon and statute erupted in the sky over the Revered Ancient mainland. The godly sea was rejected, piece by piece, bit by bit, ultimately collapsing into mist that scattered in all directions.

Within that mist, Xu Qing hovered, looking up into the dome of heaven. His thoughts were clear now. He had faced an unknown enemy on the way back, and if he hadn’t been fully prepared, it would have been extremely difficult.

That encounter had left Xu Qing with some very deep suspicions. That was especially true considering that, although this mysterious enemy had taken steps to conceal their identity, Xu Qing had noticed a few clues.

That was why, after arriving in Revered Ancient, he had not used very many techniques to fight the ancient immortal, but had immediately gone into a battle of daos and canon. His goal had been to push his opponent to the limit as quickly as possible, and force him to sever his connections to Revered Ancient. But also, Xu Qing had wanted to see... who was backing the ancient immortal, and how powerful of an organization they represented.

Part of his reason for doing all that was because of the mysterious attack on the way back. That unknown enemy had obviously wanted to kill him, but upon realizing that wasn’t possible, had tried to delay him.

Given all of the evidence, Xu Qing had begun to strongly suspect that the person behind this huge catastrophe for Revered Ancient probably wasn’t just the ancient immortal. If he didn’t find out who was operating behind the scenes, then it would lead to potential calamities down the line. That was what had led to the dao fighting earlier.

Moments ago, when the ancient immortal severed all of his achievements and virtues, and had lost his place as an immortal, Xu Qing had detected something stirring behind him.

That was why he hadn’t hesitated to unleash The Human World Sword. And what was revealed was that drop of water! All of these thoughts swirled in Xu Qing’s mind, turning into something astonishingly cold in his eyes.

So, it was you all along!

He had previously speculated that one of the God Paragons of the Ninth Star Ring was the culprit, although he had been unsure which one it was. Now he knew who was behind everything.

That God Lord you sent is just a clone....

Looking up into the starry sky, he blurred into motion, becoming a streak of silver that shot upward. He moved with incredible speed, reaching the height of the sky. There, he spoke, his words echoing throughout Revered Ancient.

“Return to me, god clone!” His words echoed out, building up into something like the crack of heavenly thunder....

He took a step forward.

Is that... a planet?

Xu Qing’s pupils constricted further as he closely observed what was happening.

This guy doesn’t just come with the machinations of God Paragons. He has assets even more mysterious than that! And almost all of those assets are directly connected to the Revered Ancient mainland....

He just let the God Lord’s eyes open. Meanwhile, inside Xu Qing’s mind, magical techniques combined to form a divine ability.

It belongs to someone else, but I can use it as a frame of reference to make... my own divine ability.

Then he hoisted the altar up! The chains from Golden Crow bound the frame to the altar, then swayed beneath it.
