“Xu Qing, I helped your daoist partner! I can still help you! With me around, she won’t suffer the effects of the curse! I know what you’re capable of but, I can... I can substitute for her in tribulations! You know that Ancient Spirits have bloodline tribulations. I can stand in for her!!”

Emperor Ancient Spirit’s eye shivered as the pressure crushed down. For a moment, it seemed that his line of reasoning was working, as the pressure eased up slightly.

But before he could breathe a sigh of relief, Xu Qing’s other hand shot out. To Emperor Ancient Spirit’s astonishment, Xu Qing’s hand latched down onto a spot right in front of the eye. The pupil of the eye constricted.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered with cold light. As his hand clenched down, a golden thread appeared that no one had noticed before. Bizarrely, it both existed and didn’t exist, at the same time. One end was attached to Emperor Ancient Spirit’s eyes, while the other... stretched off into the darkness and gloom.

So, it’s just as I predicted.

Xu Qing had guessed that the reason Emperor Ancient Spirit had survived for so long wasn’t just due to his own unique nature. He had outside help. Perhaps Emperor Ancient Spirit’s personhood was what made him a good choice of a pawn.

This hair makes it clear who the backer really is.

As Xu Qing gripped the thread, he sent divine will through it and into the darkness. The gloom of the Spirit Abyss became illuminated as if with heavenly fire, allowing him to see everything clearly. It was easy to lock down on what was at the other end of the thread.

In the shortest of moments, Xu Qing’s divine will saw what existed in the depths of the Spirit Abyss. There was a beast lurking in the mist there. It was a beast that looked somewhat like a golden lizard. And the beast was asleep.

However, when Xu Qing’s divine will approached, the beast’s eyes opened. The gaze made contact with Xu Qing’s divine will. Formless fluctuations erupted in the Spirit Abyss. Boundless curse power emerged from the awakened beast.

Īt was actually the fourth God Paragon that existed outside of Revered Ancient! Of course, what was manifested here was only a stream of divine will. Even still, when īt and Xu Qing faced off, the void shattered, causing rifts to fly out through the Spirit Abyss.

Xu Qing ignored that, and instead looked coldly at the beast. The golden beast looked back just as coldly.

“Give me that Ancient Spirit behind you and I’ll leave.”

The golden beast’s godly voice caused all wills, souls, and everything else to tremble. The words even caused Xu Qing’s canon and statute to tremble. After all, this was the divine will of a God Paragon!

That said, Xu Qing was by no means unfamiliar with God Paragons. Despite how his canon and statute were affected, the fire of a lamp ignited in front of him.

Then came the lampshade. Xu Qing grasped the lamp and held it aloft. The lamp had been crafted from the eye of a God Paragon, and that eye now opened. Boundless golden light turned into a vast sea that rushed toward the beast. That one glance caused the void to shatter, and brought signs of destruction from every direction.

The golden beast shook violently as cracks spread out over hīm. The beast even backed up, gaze cold. Īt looked at the lamp, then at Xu Qing. As the beast backed up, the surrounding air collapsed. In the end, īt chose to give up on the idea of probing for further information, and instead decided to leave Revered Ancient and go back to hīs true form.

But....

Before Xu Qing drew that line of demarcation, he would have let the beast leave without interfering. But he had made that line, and the beast had chosen to stay. Therefore, īt was not going to leave casually.... If īt succeeded, it would obviously cause irreparable damage to the credibility of Xu Qing’s earlier ultimatum! Regardless of which angle he looked at it, Xu Qing knew he had to act. He needed the outsiders to understand the ramifications of choosing to stay.

Therefore, he lifted the lamp, looked at the departing golden beast, and calmly said, “Entropy!”

The lamp vibrated, and it was just barely possible to hear something like labored breathing from the ancient past. It was the departing breath of the former God Paragon of the Fifth Star Ring.

When the sound echoed into the void, the eye in the lamp emitted a golden light that was vastly superior to anything from before. In the blink of an eye, the entire surrounding void turned golden!

Next, the entire world turned golden. That breath affected the void. The mist. All things... including the beast that was trying to leave.

The beast shivered. Hē could sense... the godly authority of a God Paragon!

So-called entropy was the process all things went through, a transformation from order into chaos. But by tapping into that godly authority and using the bolstering aspect of it, any and all things could be transformed.

The previously pitch-black Spirit Abyss was now full of golden light. It was a world of gold.

Within that golden glow, the might of godly authority radiated from the God Paragon’s eye in the lamp. It surged like mighty waves atop a mighty sea.

Wherever it passed, all things disappeared within the golden color. They weren’t destroyed. Nor were they dismantled in the way that Xu Qing’s canon and statute would do. They were reduced over and over again in a gradual process. It was a process that could not be reversed without godly authority. All things transformed. Every life form, all auras, whether they were illusory or corporeal, and regardless of where they existed in space or time. Everything was reduced, and was thus foreordained to disappear.

Naturally speaking, that included the golden beast. Īt was a God Paragon, but was not present in īts true form. Īt was only a manifestation of divine will, and was thus very limited. Despite possessing God Paragon personhood, hē was up against the personhood of another God Paragon, and therefore, was unable to hold out for long.

After all, the eye of the God Paragon didn’t just have its own power. It had been blessed and bolstered by Grandmaster Bai. Because of that, this lamp was the most dangerous tool at Xu Qing’s disposal.

As the light spread, the golden beast was soon the only thing remaining in the area. However, īts divine will manifestation was slowly but surely fading away. Finally, īt turned and looked at Xu Qing.

“You,” he said coldly, “will eventually have to leave this place.”

Then the golden beast’s eyes closed, and īt disappeared within the golden light. Īt had been erased.

Thus, the beast was driven away. The only thing that remained was the echo of hīs voice, which was already fading away.

Xu Qing’s gaze was cold. He knew what was implied by the beast’s words. Even with the lamp made from the eye of a God Paragon, he was as far removed from the God Paragon’s true form as the land was from the sky. It wasn’t even worth mentioning trying to fight such a being.

The only reason the four God Paragons of the Ninth Star Ring had agreed to a compromise, and were allowing Xu Qing to do what he wished with Revered Ancient, was Eminent Desolation. Thēy feared Eminent Desolation, and didn’t dare to show up in thēir true forms. They would only send in clones, arrange for subordinates, and use divine will to manipulate things.

Thankfully, Xu Qing’s battle prowess was sufficient to allow him to wipe out the divine will that thēy had sent. That was why thēy had chosen to just wait and see how things would play out.

But as the golden beast had said, eventually Xu Qing would have to go out into the open. If he ever left the vicinity of Revered Ancient, then he wouldn’t have the threat of Eminent Desolation to keep him safe. And then the God Paragons would have many ways to see him dead.

While it was true that Xu Qing had the karma of Eminent Desolation on him, and had even provoked Eminent Desolation into action in the Fourth Star Ring, the God Paragons didn’t need to personally take action against him. They could easily send hosts of God Lords to fight on their behalf.

“Will I go out...?”

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed as he put the lamp away. When the godly might of the lamp vanished, he shivered, and his face seemed to go slightly pale. Even being in a state of fusion between immortal and god, using that treasure was difficult. Every time he did... it was extremely draining. And this time, he had used a lot of the godly authority of the God Paragon.

As soon as the golden beast was gone, he retracted his will and tightly sealed the God Paragon lamp.

Not a bit of golden light remained in the Spirit Abyss. Everything was dark again. However, this time, that darkness was complete. Things had played out in a very neat and tidy manner. As of now, nothing existed in the Spirit Abyss, other than the trembling, decomposing snake.

Xu Qing had controlled the golden light so that the eyes of Emperor Ancient Spirit were unaffected.

Zhou Zhengli and the others flew out from the world atop the snake. They had been able to sense everything that was happening, and it left them in even greater awe of Xu Qing. Even Sir Star Ring quietly bowed his head.

If that was true of them, there was little need to mention Emperor Ancient Spirit. He saw that the Spirit Abyss was empty, and the terrifying entity he had dealt with in the past was gone. The astonishment and fear in his eyes was evident.

When Xu Qing saw the huge snake trembling, and looked at the fear in Emperor Ancient Spirit’s eyes, he shook his head. “It must have taken a lot of courage for Emperor Ancient Spirit to conquer Revered Ancient all those years ago. But in the end, he failed and perished. As for you... you’re just a manifestation of his obsession, which ended up being used by a God Paragon. That’s how you stayed alive. Unfortunately, you are not the Emperor Ancient Spirit of the past.”

Emperor Ancient Spirit said nothing, but his eyes were full of bitterness. Eventually, he closed those eyes. He knew that he couldn’t fight back. And he had to admit that what Xu Qing said was true. He really was not the Emperor Ancient Spirit of the past. He had been woken up by an external force, and had been struggling on death’s door the entire time he lurked in the Spirit Abyss.

“However,” Xu Qing continued, “you have the same personhood as before. Maybe you are a clone, but you’re connected to Revered Ancient.... You’re the manifestation of an obsession focused on possessing a heavenly dao, right...? Well, today I’m going to make you into a heavenly dao.”

Xu Qing reached out, grabbed Emperor Ancient Spirit’s eyes, as well as the huge snake, and then teleported away. He reappeared in the sky over Revered Ancient. The words he had just spoken had understandably caused all of Emperor Ancient Spirit’s eyes to open wide with shock.

Xu Qing looked up. “For Revered Ancient cultivators, the path beyond Smoldering God has been severed. It is only because of very unique and special legacies that Imperial Sovereigns can appear. It’s because Eminent Desolation devoured so many heavenly daos that the dao of cultivators became incomplete.”

Xu Qing’s eyes suddenly glittered coldly. “Heavenly daos!”

The words he spoke surpassed any heavenly daos or heavenly voices. They filled Revered Ancient. Rumbling sounds echoed out as figures began to materialize in front of him. Some looked human, some were other species. They were the fragmented remains of the heavenly daos of Revered Ancient. Most were in shabby condition, with scattered auras.

“Today, I carry out a righteous bestowal. Going forward, the ninety-nine eyes of Emperor Ancient Spirit are ninety-nine heavenly daos of Revered Ancient!”

Xu Qing’s voice thrummed with the power of righteous bestowal. As soon as it echoed out, the destiny aura of Revered Ancient surged, and auspicious signs proliferated in all directions. The bedraggled heavenly daos bowed their heads, stepped back, and yielded their personhood.

Xu Qing’s gaze fell onto Emperor Ancient Spirit. Emperor Ancient Spirit’s eyes glimmered with excitement.

“Many thanks, Lord Revered!”

The eyes spread out and sped toward the snake. When they merged, the huge snake shivered, and ninety-nine wounds appeared on its surface. Within each wound, an eye developed. The eyes opened. Howling, the snake rose up into the sky. Each eye was a dao, and combined, they formed ninety-nine heavenly daos that became part of Revered Ancient.

Revered Ancient trembled.

Countless species could sense what was happening. And the scattered cultivators stuck in late Smoldering God gained sudden enlightenment that filled them with excitement. They now sensed the tug of the path to Imperial Sovereign! It was all because of Emperor Ancient Spirit’s personhood and cultivation base!

“Unfortunately,” Xu Qing said softly, “the heavenly daos are still incomplete. There should be a full hundred.”

His gaze... left Sea-Sealing County. In the lands beyond was something that mortals would see as a huge infant, grinning as it rushed toward Xu Qing. Unfortunately, it was covered with many gaping wounds. Those were thanks to the contamination brought by the ancient immortal.

Xu Qing’s gaze softened as he looked at the infant. “Let the damaged daos return!”

As his voice spread, the damaged daos that had given up their personhood became streaks of light that shot toward the infant. One by one, they fused with it. The infant’s aura grew stronger and stronger, all while the wounds began to close.

In the end, the infant glowed with many-colored light. And it began to mature. As Xu Qing watched, it turned into a boy of about six or seven years old. He had a fair face and skin as white as snow. Overall, he looked like pure, glistening jade. His eyes were as black as lacquer, and they glittered like deep pools of water, or like dazzling stars, making him seem pure, without a spot of evil within him. Like a spring flower, he was a delight just to look at.

It seemed like he was the embodiment of auspiciousness. Slowly standing up, he clasped his small hands together and bowed.

“Hello, Father.”

Xu Qing smiled. "You were originally formless, descended due to a destined opportunity, born as a heavenly dao, and endowed with the personhood of an ancient dao. Today, I carry out a righteous bestowal. You are now the number one heavenly dao of Revered Ancient! You command the ninety-nine daos of the Ancient Spirit! Going forward... you shall safeguard Revered Ancient!”

Xu Qing's voice carried the might of canon and statute. Bolstered by destiny aura, it caused Revered Ancient to tremble. Countless species could sense the righteous bestowal of the new heavenly dao. Daybreak light spread, bright and auspicious.

Within that light, the child nodded at Xu Qing, looking like the picture of earnestness. “I shall obey you, Father. I will definitely safeguard Revered Ancient. As long as I remain, Revered Ancient will remain. But even if I do not remain, I will still do everything in my power to make sure that Revered Ancient does remain.”

Xu Qing inclined his head.

The child took a deep breath then looked in another direction, toward his second father. He bowed. freewebnovel.com

Then he floated up into the sky, surrounded by dazzling, auspicious light. As the ninety-nine Ancient Spirit daos bowed their heads, the child stepped into the personhood of the number one heavenly dao of Revered Ancient!

As it happened, the natural laws of Revered Ancient thrummed.

The heavenly daos of Revered Ancient were reconstructed, whereupon... one eternal dao and ninety-nine additional daos allowed the path of cultivation to continue. It was a truly virtuous achievement for Revered Ancient. It meant hope for countless species. The path of cultivation had been extended!

Emperor Ancient Spirit, who had once possessed Summer Immortal personhood, brought an obsession that was like a bright lamp in the darkness that covered all species. The fog of confusion was dispelled, and the lamp lit the way to the other shore of pāramitā.

There are a few more things to take care of.

Xu Qing looked out over the lands briefly, then took a step forward. Zhou Zhengli kept pace with him.

Time passed. Three days went by. During that time, Xu Qing went to several locations. For one thing, he visited all of the species who worshiped gods. And he went to other places where evidence existed of outside influence. In the end, he extracted all the pawns, one by one.

By the time he finished with that effort, his immortal-god fusion had reached the limit, and he couldn’t maintain it anymore. On the evening of the third day, he ended the fusion at the foot of the Ghost Emperor mountain.

The god clone became separate and took in all the godhood. To some extent, his god clone... was really a clone of Eminent Desolation. Hē was made from the flesh and blood of Eminent Desolation, and also had Eminent Desolation’s godhood. Although hē was still closely tied to Xu Qing, that connection couldn’t be considered completely reliable.

Because of that, Xu Qing didn’t have hīm return to the necropolis. Instead, he sent hīm into the interior of Revered Ancient.

As the evening light shone down on his immortal body, he stood there looking up at the looming Ghost Emperor mountain. Zhou Zhengli and the others stood behind him silently.

Ahead of him on the mountain... was a person. He sat cross-legged on the summit of the mountain, his clothes a bit dirty, his expression haggard, his eyes closed as he sought enlightenment.

“Third Sib,” Xu Qing said softly.

This person was Master Seventh’s third apprentice, who was Xu Qing’s Third Elder Brother! When catastrophe struck Revered Ancient years ago, Master Seventh went into seclusion, Xu Qing left the mainland, Erniu went to Brilliant Heaven, and Second Elder Sister took charge of Seven Blood Eyes. As for Third Sib... he went to the Ghost Emperor mountain.

He had sat down cross-legged on the summit, and had meditated there for half of a sixty-year-cycle. He had hoped to use the power of his past lives to defend the people he cared about.

After all, he was the reincarnation of the Ghost Emperor! As a result, he had a deep connection to the Ghost Emperor mountain.... Master Seventh was aware of that, of course. And when Xu Qing thought back, he realized there had been clues pointing to that fact all along.

Long ago, the Ghost Emperor passed away into meditation in Emperor-Receiving Prefecture, whereupon his three spiritual souls became the spirits and his seven physical souls became fiends. As for his spirit power, it dispersed into his surroundings, providing nourishment to all living beings in Emperor-Receiving Prefecture. Obviously, his life essence still existed.

Whether it was because of Third Sib’s reincarnation or because of outside forces, he was destined to return to Emperor-Receiving Prefecture eventually. He had a rough youth, and developed a powerful animosity, but eventually one of his servants got him to Seven Blood Eyes. That was when he became the third apprentice of Master Seventh.

Of course, there was a gap between his past life and his present life. Truly returning, and truly tapping into the power of his past life, was not going to be an easy task. The three spiritual souls had not returned, and the seven physical souls weren’t cooperating. His life essence... was just life essence, nothing more.

And as a result, even after meditating on the Ghost Emperor mountain for about thirty years, Third Sib had not yet succeeded.

If Xu Qing had not returned, then when catastrophe struck Revered Ancient again, it was possible his backer, the black pagoda of the Ninth Star Ring, would have helped him to fuse with his past life. Then he would have become the black pagoda’s most powerful pawn. However, if that had happened, he would no longer have been himself.

But Xu Qing did come back, and he did draw the line of demarcation. He ended the tribulation of the ancient immortal, and the black pagoda became the only one of the four God Paragons to sever karmic connections to all pawns in Revered Ancient.

Because of that, Third Sib... became free. When Xu Qing spoke, Third Sib slowly opened his eyes.

“Fourth Sib...” he said in a hoarse voice.

Xu Qing had never been as close with his Third Sib as he had been with his Eldest Brother or Second Elder Sister. What stuck out in Xu Qing’s mind the most was the incident with the Merfolk princess back in Seven Blood Eyes. Xu Qing chased the princess all the way to Third Sib’s dharmaboat. She ran right into the gentle Third Sib’s embrace, whereupon he killed her mercilessly.[1]

It had been a big shock to Xu Qing. Because of that, his guard had gone up, and he had always done his best to avoid getting close to Third Sib.

Thinking about the past, and taking into account the present, Xu Qing couldn’t help but sigh inwardly. He took a step forward, placing him right in front of the haggard-looking Third Sib on the top of the mountain.

“Third Sib,” he said, “do you need some help fusing with your past life?”

A look of bewilderment glimmered in Third Sib’s eyes. A moment later, he shook his head. “Do you want to hear my story, Fourth Sib?”

Xu Qing nodded.

Third Sib produced a jug of alcohol, took a sip, then said, “I was born here in Emperor-Receiving Prefecture.... But back then, I didn’t know about my connection to the Ghost Emperor.

“And yet, I could always hear a faint voice calling out to me.... It was calling me to here, to this very mountain. As I grew older, the call grew stronger. And eventually, I started to get the feeling... that the mountain was actually me.

“When Master went into seclusion, the call grew more urgent. That’s why I came here. When both you and Eldest Brother went missing, I assumed you were trying to help Master in some way. I wanted to do the same....

“So I came here hoping to fuse with the mountain. During the process... I saw a black pagoda. The black pagoda told me that the call I’d heard all those years wasn’t from the Ghost Emperor mountain. Hē said that it was hīm. Hē was calling to me because hē wanted my soul, my flesh, my blood, and everything about me. Hē said that if I agreed, hē could keep Seven Blood Eyes safe. I agreed.

“The truth is that I wasn’t totally sure if the Ghost Emperor mountain and my present life had any connection. But I wanted to try. With the help of that black pagoda, I started to fuse with the mountain. It was a very long process. And in the end, Fourth Sib, I saw you establish that line of demarcation in the starry sky.

“I saw the black pagoda sever the connection to me, giving me my freedom.... And yet....”

Third Sib looked up at Xu Qing. “The moment the connection was severed, I found that the voice that had been calling to me from my youth... was still there! The voice wasn’t coming from the black pagoda. But I could also tell it wasn’t coming from the Ghost Emperor mountain either. The black pagoda had deceived me. The voice... is coming from that direction....”

He pointed to the north. “There’s someone waiting there for me... someone who’s been waiting for a long time....”

When Xu Qing saw Third Sib pointing to the north, his heart thumped in his chest. That was the direction of the Supreme Beginning Netherflight Pillar, as well as... the ghast hollow!

“You asked me if I want to fuse with the Ghost Emperor. Well, Fourth Sib, I don’t. I want to go there, to the source of the call... to see the person calling to me.” Third Sib looked at Xu Qing.

“Okay.” Xu Qing waved his hand, and everything rippled and blurred. An instant later... he and Third Elder Brother vanished from atop the Ghost Emperor mountain.

Astonishingly, when they reappeared, they were on the ice plains north of Emperor-Receiving Prefecture. They were hovering in the air. Snow drifted in the cold wind as the Supreme Beginning Netherflight Pillar rose in front of them. The immense pillar began to tremble, and faint magical symbols began to glow on its surface. Eventually, the entire Supreme Beginning Netherflight Pillar was glowing brightly.

However, Third Sib didn’t seem interested in the transformation to the pillar. His attention was focused on something below. Put precisely, he was looking at... the spot where the pillar connected to the ground! That was the entrance to the ghast hollow!

“All of these years, the voice calling to me was in there....”

He instinctively reached out toward the Supreme Beginning Netherflight Pillar. Whether it was because of the thirty years he had spent trying to fuse with the Ghost Emperor mountain, or because of the interference of the God Paragon, in the end, Third Sib had developed a close connection to the pillar.

Rumbling sounds echoed out from the pillar. To the shock of the cultivators in the tent city, the massive Supreme Beginning Netherflight Pillar began to slowly rise into the air. The ice plains quaked! Higher and higher the pillar rose until it emerged from the ground! Powerful winds blasted out, sending tents flying and cultivators tumbling. The local swordsages were visibly astonished, and flew up into the air to see what was happening.

As the Supreme Beginning Netherflight Pillar rose into the air, a pitch-black cave appeared. That cave... was the ghast hollow! Frigid energy pulsed out of it, as well as the sound of a woman singing.

“In past lives forlorn, always reborn, sever lovesickness and endlessly mourn....

“In a life of hesitation, in a future of frustration, who is it that waits for me in reincarnation....”[2]

It was sad and beautiful singing that sounded like mournful weeping. It was a melody that mixed the regrets and reluctance of the past life with the confusion and loneliness of the present life. Every single word contained lovesickness and desolation, and it swirled in the cold, snowy wind like long, black hair that could never be cut, until it formed a most beautiful and disconsolate image.

It was almost possible to see into the past, to a love now covered with the dust of time. As that love crumbled in the wind of time, it left behind faint sadness lingering in the heart.

And the song continued....

Three lives’ dreams cannot memory sway, but regrets will drift in the breeze unfailing.

Four lifetimes’ pain stings, obsession swirled, the Bridge of Helplessness is soaked by wailing.

Five lifetimes’ of waiting, destiny gone, only this cave shows my love’s unveiling.

Six lifetimes’ lone cry, the old dream fades and the beauty of youth is unavailing....

1. The Merfolk incident was in chapter 98. Back then, we knew Third Sib as Third Highness. ☜

2. This song first appeared in chapter 364. It was repeated in a few subsequent chapters, notably 676 and 956. ☜

As the song drifted about, Third Sib’s expression became one of bewilderment.

“The black pagoda tricked me. It made me think the call was coming from the Ghost Emperor mountain.... Yet all along, the call was coming from here.... But I’ve been to the Supreme Beginning Netherflight Pillar before, and I didn’t feel anything like this....”

Third Sib’s voice trembled in the wind. Xu Qing realized now what had played out. It was all thanks to that black pagoda. Hē had wanted Third Sib to fuse with the Ghost Emperor. It wasn’t just a situation of the pagoda trying to trick Third Sib by making it seem like the call came from the mountain.

Xu Qing wasn’t sure why the black pagoda valued the Ghost Emperor so much.... Although the Ghost Emperor had been strong, that was only from the perspective of low-level cultivators. To truly strong cultivators, the Smoldering God level wasn’t very impressive.

There must be another, deeper reason....

Meanwhile, Third Elder Brother seemed to be in a daze as he started walking toward the ghast hollow. He didn’t stop at the edge. He went right in.

Xu Qing followed. In the darkness of the ghast hollow, the singing became clearer. Paper money drifted everywhere. The mutagen levels were very high.

Third Sib didn’t seem to care about that. He ignored the infection of the mutagen and the filtering paper money. He moved down... faster and faster. His heart was also beating faster and faster. The waiting that had stretched from life to life seemed to be culminating right here and now. Lost memories and shadows of the past seemed to slip through time, shine through reincarnation, and form within his mind. A look of excitement was building on his face, and he was physically shaking.

Upon seeing this, Xu Qing found himself thinking about someone.

It was a person he had known in the scavenger basecamp in South Phoenix, just outside that forbidden region. A similar expression had appeared on his face when he heard a certain song and saw a loved one. He had looked excited, and had even started trembling.[1]

“Sergeant Thunder...” Xu Qing murmured. He continued to follow after Third Sib, clearing the mutagen for him and enabling him to move faster and faster.

Eventually, deep in the darkness of the ghast hollow, a red lamp became visible. And then... Third Sib saw a log cabin. It looked very dilapidated, as if it had existed for countless years of time, to the point where the wood was starting to decay. The structure was pentagonal, and each corner had a gray iron chain attached to it that stretched out to the wall of the tunnel.

On the corners of the pentagonal cabin, where the chains connected, were terrifying zombies. One of them was dripping wet and severely decayed. It had a tattered black robe that looked like it had existed for countless years. Another had its hands at its own abdomen. It was in the middle of ripping apart its own belly, revealing the abdominal cavity beneath. There were no organs inside.

The third zombie was different from the other two. It had a red vine wrapped around its waist. The ends of the vine were held tightly in the zombie’s hands, as if it had tied the vine around itself and pulled it tight to end its own life.

The fourth and fifth were equally bizarre. The fourth was the skeletal remains of a child, lain beneath an unmarked gravestone. The fifth... had been burned. It... was familiar to Xu Qing. It wasn’t the zombie that Xu Qing had fought here. Instead, it was... the dao child Zhang Siyun, who had died here.[2]

“Metal to dissect,” Xu Qing said softly. “Wood to strangle. Water to drown. Fire to immolate. Earth to bury.”

Then he looked at the log cabin suspended in midair.

Faint red light filled the cabin, casting the shadow of a woman on the paper window. The paper was torn in spots, making it possible to see a woman inside, dressed in a red opera costume. She sat at the window, her fair hand extended as she tossed out paper money. The paper money scattered, caught up in a cold wind as it flowed outward and upward.

But then, all of a sudden, her hand stopped moving. The singing stopped.

“You... came...” she said, her voice soft and full of bitterness.

Third Sib shivered as he looked at the shadow on the paper window. “I’m too late....”

Third Sib tried to open the door of the cabin, but it didn’t budge.

“It’s fine... just sit outside and talk to me....”

Third Sib nodded and sat down outside the log cabin. As he looked at the shadow on the paper window, his mind filled with vague memories. A love that lasted seven lifetimes had finally reached this point. However, all he could remember was a feeling. He did not remember who this person was.

Xu Qing looked on, sighing inwardly. He did not know the story of Third Sib and this woman from the ghast hollow. But he did know why the two of them could not truly reunite.

Her shadow on the paper window was beautiful. But in reality, she was a zombie. This was an altar. A ceremony. And originally, that ceremony didn’t involve five zombies. It needed six! She was the sixth zombie, a zombie who had drowned to death in love.

Right now, the two of them... needed time alone.

Xu Qing’s gaze shifted to what was beneath the log cabin. No other person could see, but he could. At the very bottom of the ghast hollow was an eye that was currently trembling and refusing to open. Years ago, that eye put immense pressure on Xu Qing. In fact, it had almost killed him. Were it not for the outside help he had received, he would have ended up mutating and dying. But now, that eye was puny as far as he was concerned.

“So, you’re from Brilliant Heaven,” he said softly. He could sense the same type of bloodline fluctuations as Crown Prince Golden Crow.

He reached out. The trembling eye of the god instantly shrank down to the size of a fist, then flew into his palm. The golden eye trembled violently. All Xu Qing did was put the eye away. Without a source, the mutagen levels in the ghast hollow immediately started to drop.

The dilapidated log cabin gradually began to show signs of life. He looked at the woman in the cabin, then Third Sib. Then he headed back up the tunnel.

Just before he was about to leave, he stopped and looked at the tunnel wall. A trembling figure was there, looking at him. It was the centipede woman who had saved him all those years ago.[3]

Xu Qing’s gaze softened. He waved his right hand, and sent some immortal essence flowing into the centipede woman, which rebuilt her foundation. The woman shivered from head to toe. When she looked up again, Xu Qing was gone.

***

The snowy wind still blew. Time passed. Snowflakes fell. Xu Qing was done putting Revered Ancient in order, and would no longer make casual public appearances.

Humankind had risen to prominence. Under the leadership of Empress Summer Departure, many species flocked to their side, even various species who worshiped gods. Most of the gods decided to stay in hiding. One exception was among the Firemoon Darkheaven people. Of course, there were still people inclined to rebel. After all, Revered Ancient was full of infiltrators. Many were from other parts of the Ninth Star Ring, but there were even forces from more distant star rings. Whenever outside agents and pawns were discovered, Zhou Zhengli and the others would quickly deal with them. Things went very smoothly. Revered Ancient was essentially united at this point.

And yet, even as those things happened, Xu Qing didn’t spend time on reunions with old friends. Together with a very excited Erniu, he... took a trip to what lay sealed beneath the imperial capital of humankind. It was... the entrance to Brilliant Heaven!

With the exception of the Heaveneater Region, there was nowhere in Revered Ancient that could pose any threat or obstacle to Xu Qing. The time had come to take care of Brilliant Heaven....

Besides, his Eldest Brother’s true form was there.

As they stood at the sealed entrance, Erniu proudly said, “Let me tell you, Little Ah Qing, you might be a badass, but your Eldest Brother is a badass in Brilliant Heaven!”

Even as the words left his mouth, the person standing next to them suddenly smacked Erniu on the side of his head.

Glaring, Master Seventh said, “You? A badass? If you’re such a badass why didn’t you get out of here on your own instead of squeezing out some lame clone?”

Master Seventh had come along for the trip to Brilliant Heaven. Ignoring Erniu, who looked like his feelings were hurt, he turned to look kindly at Xu Qing. From the kindness in his eyes, it was as if Xu Qing was the only apprentice that he had ever had in his entire life.

“I’m very familiar with Brilliant Heaven, my little apprentice. With me to lead the way, things will go very smoothly. Those old codgers couldn’t actually kill the Brilliant Heaven god emperor back then, so they resorted to a sealing.... I doubt hē’s dead. In fact, based on my calculations, the god emperor probably isn’t at the God Lord level anymore, although hē’s probably close.”

Nodding, Xu Qing bowed. “Thank you for your trouble, Master.” freewebnovel.com

“Oh, it’s no problem at all! Years ago I took you down to that necropolis, and today, I’ll take you to Brilliant Heaven!” Master Seventh flashed a very benevolent smile.

Erniu clearly did not like being ignored so obviously. “Master,” he said tartly, “you’re too biased. Actually, you took both me and little Ah Qing to that necropolis. Yet you didn’t even mention me just now!

“Also... I too am very familiar with Brilliant Heaven. I’m even more familiar with it than you are! Have you ever even seen that god emperor? Well listen to me, you old codger, I personally laid eyes on the exact spot where the god emperor is sealed. And when I did—”

Erniu let out a loud yelp as Master Seventh viciously kicked him through the entrance. “You little rat bastard! Since you like calling me codger, then going forward, you can forget about calling me Master. You’re familiar with Brilliant Heaven? You go in and lead the way!”

Erniu’s scream echoed out as he tumbled into the entrance. Ignoring him, Master Seventh smiled broadly, reached out, and clasped Xu Qing’s hand.

“Let’s go, my little apprentice.”

A brown wind swept through a dark sky and an overgrown wilderness landscape. It carried death and emptiness. Dust swirled. As faint light drifted down from above, it seemed like ancient time was being crushed by the mottle shadows.

The entire world seemed like it had been cursed with an aura of despair. The sky was like a massive, dark cloth covering everything, but hovering on the brink of collapse. Flows of mutagen swept through the air, drifting with the wind. They were like living tentacles, piercing everything. It was so strong it seemed to be on the verge of becoming corporeal, and in fact, in many places, it was a thick mist that permeated the surroundings.

The lands had long since lost any traces of life, and looked like they were decomposing. Deep gullies were visible everywhere, like vicious mouths howling against fate.

That said, life did exist. Within the gullies were tenacious plants that pulsed with evil energy, perhaps due to their nature, or perhaps due to the environment and the ever present mutagen. Their branches were twisted and distorted, making them look like bitterly struggling animals. And they were covered with thorns, some of which glittered with bizarre light that was a clear warning to stay away.

They had very bizarre leaves. Some were wide like woven fans, but covered with numerous holes, as if some unknown creature had gnawed away at them. Others were long and thin like swords, but with serrated edges. As they swayed in the breeze, they seemed sharp enough to cause serious wounds to anyone who touched them.[1]

Occasionally, hulking beasts could be seen in the dangerous landscape, and they pulsed with godliness. They looked even stranger than the plants. Some were covered with innumerable cold and ruthless eyes that seemed capable of seeing all hidden things in the world. Some were covered with scales as tough as iron, which glowed faintly in the darkness. Every step such beasts took left deep tracks in the land, and caused muffled booms to echo out. Others had immense wings that caused cold winds to blow when they beat, winds full of decay and mutagen.

And yet, what was most eye-catching in the bizarre wastelands... was not any of those things. It was... the numerous immense temples that dotted the landscape.

The temples seemed extremely primeval, as if they had been standing in the same spot since the most ancient of times. Though they were situated haphazardly, they all conformed to the same style. Their walls were made of massive stone slabs covered with cryptic, mysterious symbols. The symbols seemed to contain life of their own, and would pulse with faint light, making it seem like they were breathing. They had immense doors covered with complicated patterns and designs. And though the designs were all different, at the top of each design was a vertical symbol that described light! It was as if light... was being worshiped by all of these temples!

This place was called Brilliant Heaven! It existed beneath Revered Ancient, and was of corresponding size. In fact, back in history... Brilliant Heaven was the true Revered Ancient. When the cultivators came from the Deep Earth star ring, it was the first world they saw.

A decisive war ended up being fought between those cultivators and the Brilliant Heaven Godfolk. And though the cultivators paid an immense price, they ultimately achieved victory! It was a victory both sweet and deeply meaningful. It gave the cultivators the right to enter the higher star rings, and to live there in the Revered Ancient mainland that they created.

Revered Ancient became the heaven over Brilliant Heaven!

The curtain dropped on Brilliant Heaven Godfolk. Most of the gods were suppressed. The imperial clan was sealed, and their crown prince became a golden crow who atoned for the crimes of the Godfolk outside of Brilliant Heaven.

The Brilliant Heaven mainland was buried. Revered Ancient was constructed atop it.

The heavenly daos were erected, and the cultivator system became a dazzling flower blooming in the Ninth Star Ring. That was what kept Brilliant Heaven tightly sealed. As time passed, Brilliant Heaven eventually became a legend. The Brilliant Heaven Godfolk were a thing of the past.

Cultivators did not go there. Until this day!

It was a day that seemed like any other day, yet was destined to be anything but ordinary. The first thing that happened was that a howl of anguish echoed out as a figure fell from the sky. Then a deafening sound rang out as the dark sky opened up!

RUUUUUUUUMBLE!

The sound filled Brilliant Heaven, echoing to the farthest corners. It was as if a huge pair of hands had grabbed the canopy of heaven... and violently ripped it open! An incredibly massive rift appeared overhead!

Two figures emerged from the rift! The moment they appeared, the mutagen in Brilliant Heaven seethed. At the same time, an aura swept forth from the two figures, and it melted all the mutagen it touched! That was because it was an immortal aura!

Brilliant Heaven was being crushed! The moment the aura swept out, all of Brilliant Heaven was thrown into chaos.

The sky distorted. Mutagen vanished. Plants trembled. Beasts prostrated.

But most affected of all were the temples that had, only moments ago, been as silent as death. It was as if life had been poured into them. In the blink of an eye, they started shaking. From the intense rumbling sounds, it seemed as if this ancient world was waking up!

Eventually, enraged roars echoed out. The statues of the gods in the various temples were moving. Thēy pulsed with very strong auras that surpassed anything mortals could comprehend. And yet... many of the statues were trembling as if thēy couldn’t sustain the force from above. In fact, many were beginning to show signs of crumbling. The reason was all because of the two people who had appeared in the dome of heaven.

“This is none other than Brilliant Heaven!” Master Seventh said, looking around at the temples with a gaze that seemed tinged with regret. “Years ago, I came here with various Seniors... to wage war against the Brilliant Heaven Godfolk!” freewebnovel.com

Master Seventh looked at Xu Qing with a serious expression on his face. “Do not underestimate the Brilliant Heaven Godfolk. Although thēy might not be as powerful as some of the other gods... thēy possess very rare innate soul abilities. And it’s not just some of thēm. Every member of thēir species has that ability! In fact, in the years since then, I never saw anything like it among other gods.”

This information caused Xu Qing’s eyes to glitter. He had only encountered two gods who had innate soul abilities. One was God Lord Death Departure of the Fourth Star Ring, and the other was Goddess Starryeyes! The former had been devoured by Erniu, while the latter was currently in Xu Qing’s bag of holding.

“As a result, we paid a grievous price to wage war with thēm. All of the Deep Earth star ring was affected.... After the victory was won, the Seniors did a lot of research into the species. Because of my unique status, I was able to participate, so I know what they uncovered. They found... that the Brilliant Heaven mainland was fundamentally important. And it was very unique!

“In fact, back then, we suspected that Brilliant Heaven... was very likely the first planet to be born in all of the star rings! And the Brilliant Heaven Godfolk were the very first inhabitants! Why else would the broken face come here?”

Xu Qing was stunned.

Primeval motherworld?

He immediately thought back to that planet in the Fourth Star Ring. But as he considered the situation, something seemed strange.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered as he looked at Master Seventh. He could sense his Master’s personhood skyrocketing along with his battle prowess. And yet, there were no signs of canon or statute! It was as if Master Seventh, despite being an immortal, didn’t have canon!

Master Seventh could tell what Xu Qing was thinking. As he powered up, he continued to explain.

“Fourth Sib, I know you’ve been to other star rings, and you’ve met many types of cultivators. You’ve become an immortal with your own dao, which the people out there call canon. Canon is similar to godly authority, and requires a source. It can be used against various gods of the higher star rings!

“Actually, those two different paths are very similar.... They both involved gaining enlightenment of the natural laws of a higher star ring.”

Having said that, Master Seventh lifted the finger that was pointing down. As his fingertip rose upward, the rumbling from below grew more intense. It multiplied many times over, so that everything below was shaking violently. At the same time, the energy of a higher star ring began to rise up from Brilliant Heaven. It was full of something wild, complex, and primeval!

The moment Xu Qing sensed it, he felt shaken. “Is that...?”

Then, Master Seventh offered the complete explanation. “Your Master... walks yet another path used by the Seniors who came here from Deep Earth! I have no canon. That’s because my dream was not to acclimate to Brilliant Heaven. It was to upgrade Deep Earth! I never wanted to merge with Revered Ancient. “That is how we became the Immortals of Deep Earth!

Master Seventh splayed his fingers and pushed his palm down toward the lands below. Everything shook wildly.

It looked like the lands of Brilliant Heaven were going to completely collapse under the weight of the palm. And yet, they did not actually shatter. Instead, as they rocked back and forth, they emitted the energy of a higher star ring. Strands of energy proliferated, growing stronger and turning into a roiling mist that was visible to the naked eye.

As Xu Qing watched, the mist created an astonishing panorama like a mirage. It was something Xu Qing had seen before in the Summer Immortal Palace. It was... the Deep Earth star ring! He could see every world, every universe, and every location!

The moment it appeared, it swept toward Master Seventh, merged into him, and caused his energy to skyrocket! Dazzling and auspicious colors swirled into a haze around him.

Yet Xu Qing could see that this power up was actually like an illusory pagoda in the sky. It didn’t truly belong to Master Seventh. It would only do that... if the image in the mirage became true and real! Without that, it was only temporary.

“Behold an Immortal of Deep Earth!” Master Seventh said softly. “Unfortunately, as our understanding became more complete, we found that the path upward is terrifying. Brilliant Heaven was only a small factor in it all. This place was a world of gods, and Deep Earth couldn’t reach it. Our path could not be walked to the end.

“That is why my Master and his fellow daoists chose to leave. They wanted to explore the path beyond, and determine where to go next. I was left behind in Revered Ancient.” Master Seventh sighed. “As of now, I could very well be the only Immortal of Deep Earth.

Master Seventh’s eyes glittered as if with rivers of stars. Within them were all the worlds of Deep Earth. Then he lifted his hand before dropping it toward the corpse of the god emperor, which was still covered with Erniu in all of his worm forms.

Tapping into the origin of the Deep Earth star ring and using it on the outside to further the interests of Deep Earth. That was what it meant to be an Immortal of Deep Earth!

Right now, Brilliant Heaven was completely astir!

As Master Seventh waved his hand, the projection of Deep Earth shot toward the corpse of the Brilliant Heaven god emperor. As it neared, dazzling light expelled all mutagen and rejected the higher star ring energy.

However, it was very evident that the origin of Deep Earth was fundamentally not on the same level as that higher energy. The clash caused the Deep Earth energy to be constantly destroyed. And yet, at the same time, the will of Deep Earth spread. That will was formed from the combined wills of all living beings in all the universes of Deep Earth, including all those who had died in battle in the past.

The moment it appeared, heaven was shaken, and destruction spread in all directions! Brilliant Heaven was shaking.

As Xu Qing hovered in midair and watched, his mind raced. He could sense the vision and boldness of the Senior cultivators who had come from Deep Earth to Brilliant Heaven. They wanted to elevate Deep Earth into Brilliant Heaven, to thereby replace Brilliant Heaven, and allow the effects of cultivator karma to flourish.

Unfortunately... Brilliant Heaven was only a small part of the Ninth Star Ring. And the Ninth Star Ring was only one of the thirty-six higher star rings. Above Deep Earth, everything belonged to the gods. And thus, the cultivator system of old was incapable of doing anything very impressive! Simply making Revered Ancient was the limit. From ancient times until now, the Fifth Star Ring was the only place that had truly been overthrown.

As Xu Qing thoughts swirled, the Deep Earth power wielded by Master Seventh reached the corpse of the Brilliant Heaven god emperor. It did not interfere with the Erniu worms and their devouring of the flesh.

The sound could shake heaven and earth. It was... the pulsing of the god veins inside the god emperor!

At the same time, the sky in Brilliant Heaven seethed with many colors. Endless mutagen roiled in all directions, and a brilliant light swirled to converge around the corpse. It was as if the corpse was instinctively absorbing all of Brilliant Heaven to defend against the incursion of Deep Earth.

Back when Xu Qing first arrived in the Fifth Star Ring, he took them from an Imperial Sovereign. After researching them, he came to find that they held information about a taboo formation related to word usage. By cultivating it to the ultimate level, the taboo formations could be activated using only two spoken words. The reason the final limit was two words was that the formations were split into yin and yang varieties, and the taboos were split into life and death varieties. They couldn’t be combined.

Because of Xu Qing’s cultivation base, as well as the blessing of his very unique canon, plus his statute of ontology, he was able to take the formations that originally couldn’t be one, and actually make them one! He reduced the spoken word to one!

When that word was spoken, the suppressing power was formed naturally, becoming natural law, and a resonance of statute! Using it on the god emperor’s corpse made it impossible for the mutagen convergence to be intercepted. That interception was accomplished, not by blocking it and keeping it outside, but rather... by suppressing it!

As a result, the seething mutagen of Brilliant Heaven was suppressed in place by the means of one spoken word!

And thus... the streams of mutagen couldn’t move. They couldn’t even twitch, much less gather together. Naturally, that meant they couldn’t affect Erniu. The Erniu worms looked more pleased than ever as they continued with their ravenous devouring.

When that happened, the worms underwent another bizarre transformation. They split apart, causing the number of worms to increase dramatically.

At the same time, as the tearing and splitting went on, some worms reached their limit and unexpectedly transformed, turning into blue fleshy strips... that filled in the parts that had been bitten away. They became part of the corpse! The corpse was being replaced!

Ten percent. Twenty percent. Thirty percent....

Taking in the scene as a whole, more and more blue flesh was appearing on the corpse, and the same was happening on the inside!

Gradually, it reached forty percent! Erniu couldn’t have been more excited. In the end, it reached the level of fifty percent!

Half of the corpse, whether inside or out, was made of worms transformed into flesh. And that half was blue. Especially noteworthy was the left arm, which seemed to be the source. The blue skin here had already begun to crystallize. And the effects were about to spread.

The pulsing of godly veins could be heard coming from the chest, even louder and clearer than before. The strands of mutagen that Xu Qing had suppressed were now wriggling violently in an attempt to break free. Intense rumbling sounds filled the air.

“The ocean of god blood is a very special place.

In the temples that had not yet been destroyed by Zhou Zhengli and the others, gods prostrated and began to chant.

“Our emperor awakens!”

“Our emperor awakens!!”

The sound grew louder and louder, filling the sky and echoing about. Then, astonishingly, light cones began to emerge from the gaping wound that was left behind when the god emperor was beheaded. There were a total of thirty-six cones! As they intersected, they turned into a face!

It was a face that Master Seventh had seen years ago.

Then, that face which he could never possibly forget... opened its eyes! Holy golden light spilled forth, turning all heaven and earth the color gold.

The god emperor was waking up! Erniu had been used to effectuate the return. It was a special place, a special method, and a special call. Together, they were a ceremony of return!

In the moment hē woke up, the faint gleam of light in hīs chest... erupted dramatically! A seven-colored glow swirled inside, filled with boundless mystery. That light was the very same origin light that the Brilliant Heaven Godfolk worshiped! It was formless, but as the sealing of the god emperor faded... the god emperor returned, and in that seeming moment of being born again, the light glimmered again!

As the origin light shone, the parts where Erniu’s flesh had replaced the god emperor began to show signs of melting! The god emperor’s power surged, and the color blue was visibly reduced. Eventually, even the left arm lost that color. freewebnovel.com

“Catch, little Ah Qing! And then... hurry up and save me!”

As thoughts of the matter flashed through Xu Qing’s mind, he looked down at the Brilliant Heaven god emperor.

Even as he caught his breath, realization hit him. “The light worshiped by the Brilliant Heaven Godfolk really is the first ray of light that came with the birth of Brilliant Heaven. At the same time... it’s the key to opening the primeval motherworld!”

The journey into Brilliant Heaven was over.

Xu Qing left. He took the mysterious light with him, that light which was the key to opening the primeval motherworld.

He left behind the sleeping Erniu, Master Seventh, and an empty tomb. Master Seventh had built the tomb personally, not with divine abilities or magical techniques. Xu Qing had not helped him. Xu Qing observed from the side, and took note of the words inscribed on the tombstone.

“Here Lies my Respected Master, Sir Spiritmortal.”

Of course, Sir Spiritmortal was the daoist name of that old immortal from the holy lands. Master Seventh had built him a tomb for the sake of their old Master-apprentice relationship. And as he bowed in front of it, an expression of grief filled his face that sank to the depths of his soul.

***

The god emperor’s karma was erased, and Xu Qing took away the origin light that had long since been worshiped. And thus, the Brilliant Heaven Godfolk lost thēir origin.... Zhou Zhengli crushed many of them, who perished.

Xu Qing did not wipe out the survivors. Instead, he let thēm stay in Brilliant Heaven near his Eldest Brother. Erniu was fusing with the body of the god emperor. Though he was currently asleep, given what the scattered remnants of the Brilliant Heaven god emperor had said, thēy viewed him as thēir new emperor.

Eldest Brother is asleep. He needs some time before he can wake up....

Before leaving, Xu Qing stood near the empty tomb, flanked by Zhou Zhengli and the others, looking at Erniu. Something like the sunrise or sunset glimmered in his eyes, which was the eternal manifestation of the light he had absorbed. He had taken all of the light into him. He also needed some time.

Because of that, Xu Qing was already thinking of going into seclusion.

Master Seventh was also looking at Erniu. But at the same time, he found himself looking at the tomb. After a while, he sighed.

“You’re thinking of going into seclusion after you go back?” he asked.

Xu Qing nodded. “For the time being, most of the potential calamities in Revered Ancient have been dealt with. Next... I need to go visit some old friends. After that, I’ll go into seclusion to completely absorb the light that the Brilliant Heaven Godfolk worshiped. At the same time, I need to further analyze the secrets of the mysterious light. In addition... Eminent Desolation is still there, and the God Paragons are still watching. My cultivation base isn’t sufficient to deal with any of that.”

Master Seventh clasped Xu Qing’s shoulder. Looking wistful, he said, “The dao will I’ve been cultivating has reached an end point. The best I can do is to watch over Revered Ancient while you’re in seclusion. Go do what you have to do. I’ll be here while you’re gone, but I’ll send my will to the outside world.”

Xu Qing looked at his Master and could tell what he was thinking. The end of Brilliant Heaven had affected his Master mentally, and now he just wanted to be alone. Without another word, Xu Qing bowed, then became a beam of prismatic light that shot up into the dome of heaven.

Zhou Zhengli and the others also bowed to Master Seventh before following Xu Qing. As a group, they rose high into the sky before disappearing into the pathway leading to Revered Ancient. When they were gone, Brilliant Heaven became peaceful and quiet.

Master Seventh looked down from the sky, walked over to the tomb, and sat down. He produced a jug of alcohol. Taking a sip, he let the breeze tug at his long hair.

“Master...” he said softly. Years ago, his Master had left, saying that he would return. And so, Master Seventh had watched over Revered Ancient, all while cultivating a special dao will. He had used a reincarnation method to extend his life. Through many reincarnations and transmigrations, he had guarded the mainland.

All that time, he had been waiting for his Master to come back. Unfortunately... what he had been waiting for wasn’t really his Master. As the wind blew, he sank deeper and deeper into rippling memories.

***

Time passed. It had already been a month since Xu Qing left Brilliant Heaven. He spent some of that time in the imperial capital of humankind.

Thanks to the leadership of Empress Summer Departure, humankind had fully risen to prominence. As a unified force, they could move mountains, and were now unstoppable.

Since Xu Qing was the imperial tutor, he officiated over the ceremony in which Ningyan officially became the crown prince.[1]

It was a grand and auspicious occasion, but Xu Qing couldn’t help think about everything that happened in the past, and would occasionally glance at Ningyan’s belly. There was still a vine there. Years ago, Erniu had used Ningyan, sometimes as a shield, other times to smash enemies. Regardless, he had been very useful as a tool. A smile tugged at Xu Qing’s lips. [2]

As Ningyan prostrated, his heart pounded. Even after all the time he had spent processing the recent developments, he still felt like he was dreaming when in Xu Qing’s presence. The dream went on as the ceremony continued.

When the formalities were over, Xu Qing left. His next stop was the Moonrite Region.

Back at the Green Spirit Pharmacy, he met with the Heir Apparent, Princess Brightblossom, Grandpa Ninth... and of course Ling’er.

Ling’er had grown up into a slender, beautiful woman. Tears streamed down her face as she threw herself into Xu Qing’s arms. Xu Qing held her and smiled warmly. It was just like old times. Unfortunately, time would not permit Xu Qing to stay in Moonrite for long. A few days later, Ling’er reluctantly bade him farewell as he left. Before leaving, he took all of the Ancient Spirit destiny aura that he had taken from Emperor Ancient Spirit and used it to bless Ling’er. With her blood purified, she could shoulder the destiny of her species.

Finally, Xu Qing headed in the direction of the continent of South Phoenix.

On the way, he stopped by the island where Yanyan lived on the Sea of Endlessness. There, he completely removed the discarnate divine will that had infected her. As a result, Yanyan’s emotions became normal. As he worked, Yanyan looked at him with mixed emotions. The entire time, she looked like she had something to tell him, but in the end... she chose to remain silent.

In South Phoenix, Xu Qing saw several old friends.

He met with the other two apprentices of Grandmaster Bai, Tingyu and Chen Feiyuan. He gave them the gift Grandmaster Bai had entrusted to him, the seed. “Master is not dead. If you’re willing to go to him, plant this seed. On the day it blooms, the fragrance of the flower will bring you to him.”

Xu Qing also went to see Zhao Zhongheng. Times had changed, but Zhao Zhongheng had not. He was still in love with Ding Xue. In fact, after all the years that had passed, his love for her had become his dao heart. As for Ding Xue... she hadn’t changed either. Because of Xu Qing’s status, she knew he was beyond her reach. But the emotions from years ago still existed in her heart.

The Mute was the most brilliant of the friends Xu Qing visited. He was already in the great circle of Core Formation. Xu Qing well remembered how he had given him an opportunity that would lead to Nascent Soul.[3]

Then there was Zhang San, the great investor who had bet heavily on Erniu and Xu Qing. When they reunited, Zhang San was very nervous at first. But eventually he relaxed, and even told Xu Qing about his dreams and aspirations. In the coming days, he planned to travel throughout Revered Ancient.

“I’m going to expand my business to cover the entire mainland!” he said proudly.

Xu Qing smiled and wished him well.

It was raining on the morning Zhang San set sail. Xu Qing saw him off. Then he looked up into the sky.

Flame Phoenix circled above, sounding very pleased with himself as he reached out to Xu Qing with divine will. Second Elder Sister was on Flame Phoenix’s back, waving down at Xu Qing. They were planning to leave South Phoenix for a time to visit other locales. Behind them was a little bird that kept flapping its wings and snapping at Flame Phoenix’s tail. Xu Qing looked at the little bird and smiled.

As the rain fell in sheets, Xu Qing stood at the mouth of the harbor and looked over his shoulder. A young woman in a green gown stepped out of the eaves of a building. She stood beneath an oilskin umbrella, looking at him.

“Long time no see, Qing Qiu,” he said softly. This young woman was the very same girl he had first met in the scavenger basecamp all those years ago. She walked through the train toward him, and stopped in front of him.

Xu Qing extended his hand and offered her a piece of candy. Qing Qiu looked at the piece of candy for a long time. Finally, she took it and pressed it against her heart. She looked at Xu Qing for a long moment, then turned to leave.[4]

A few hundred paces away, just as she was about to disappear into the rain, her soft voice drifted back to reach his ears. “Big Bro Kid! If my brother hadn’t come to take me away from that scavenger basecamp, I might have gone to Seven Blood Eyes with you. I wonder what things would have been like if that happened....”

Xu Qing said nothing.

After a moment of silence, Qing Qiu put the candy in her mouth and vanished into the rain.

Xu Qing watched Qing Qiu leave, then strolled through the streets of Seven Blood Eyes. He passed many shops and saw many people. Some were mortals, some were cultivators. He had many memories of this place, and there were plenty of familiar locations that made him think of past events. As he reminisced, his heart gradually grew calm.

In the end, he reached the old Harbor 176. Reaching through time, he extracted his original dharmaboat and put it onto the water.[5]

He sat cross-legged in the dharmaboat, and as he felt himself bobbing up and down in the water, he closed his eyes. In that manner... he went into seclusion.

Twenty years passed. During that time, the situation in Revered Ancient changed in heaven-shaking, earth-toppling ways!

In the name of Xu Qing, Empress Summer Departure triumphantly expanded human territory to the point where it matched the extent of human lands in the days of Emperor Eastglory. And that was only what humans directly controlled. During the twenty years that had passed, humans became the top species in Revered Ancient. They controlled more than half of the mainland!

There were other areas home to either gods or ancient species, and yet... they all feared humans and didn’t dare to cause trouble. Yet they weren’t willing to bend the knee.

It was a stalemate of three parties. That was when Ling’er emerged from the Moonrite Region, accompanied by the Heir Apparent and his siblings. By means of her Ancient Spirit bloodline, she was able to give the countless ancient species of Revered Ancient a face-saving way of submitting.

For a variety of reasons, they didn’t want to bend the knee to humankind. But they viewed the Ancient Spirits differently. All of those ancient species were fine with the concept of ‘countless species’ existing in Revered Ancient. But in reality... they were all nonhumans who existed apart from the humans. And before Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity conquered Revered Ancient, it had been a nonhuman species, the Ancient Spirits, who ruled the mainland. In the end, they could agree to bend the knee to the Ancient Spirits.

And thus, the only obstacle to the complete unification of Revered Ancient were the gods. Naturally speaking, it made the most sense for gods to handle the business of gods. Therefore, Empress Summer Departure went to South Phoenix, prostrated in front of Xu Qing’s dharmaboat, and sought his counsel.

Waves rippled on the surface of the seawater, and the dharmaboat bobbed up and down. Xu Qing opened his eyes. He did not emerge from seclusion. But he did wave his hand, causing a stream of light to emerge from the dharmaboat and coalesce in front of the empress.

It turned into a clay statue. It was a statue of a fox.

As the wind blew through the harbor, the statue glittered with dazzling light. The clay became flesh, smooth and lustrous, and charming laughter rang out. Then, the bewitching Starfire appeared in the world again.

“Long time no see, Big Sis,” Starfire said, eyes shimmering flirtatiously. “Thanks for coming. If you hadn’t, that heartless meanie would have completely forgotten about me.”

The empress frowned but said nothing. With a final bow to Xu Qing’s dharmaboat, shē turned and left.

Laughing softly, Starfire looked in the direction of the Moonrite Region, eyes shining with anticipation. “First, Sun. Then, Moon. Finally, Star.... It’s time to change the rankings.”

Starfire began walking.

The first stop was, of course, the Firemoon Darkheaven people. In Firemoon lands, God Mountain trembled as a rain of clay began to fall. As the rain fell, the Firemoon Darkheavens trembled with dread. At the same time, a towering godly might descended with the rain, landing on God Mountain and turning into a godly voice.[1]

“Moonfire. Sunfire. Come out and see me!”

God Mountain trembled as Sunfire and Moonfire appeared and flew up into the sky, expressions uncertain. It wasn’t possible to go very high. Moonfire only advanced about seven paces before stopping silently with bowed head. Sunfire glowed like a dazzling sun, but despite struggling to surpass Moonfire, only advanced by a few more paces. Then the sun turned into a clay sun. After looking up with a penetrating glance, Sunfire looked down. freewebnovel.com

The laughter of the clay fox rang out in all directions. Instead of Sun, Moon, Star, the rankings were now Star, Moon, Sun.

After that, Starfire went to the locations of many other gods, and used a variety of methods to offer such gods two choices. Option one was to be destroyed. Option two was to become a subordinate god. That was how the gods were subjugated. There were some dangers, as certain sleeping gods were actually stronger than Starfire. But Master Seventh was around the entire time.

During the twenty years of Xu Qing’s secluded meditation, Master Seventh only came out of Brilliant Heaven twice. The first was to exterminate an old-timer from one of the ancient species who had a special magic to rely on. The second was to crush three gods who were half a step into the True God level.

Due to his actions, there were no deadly conflicts between nonhumans, gods, and humans. And thanks to Ling’er and Starfire taking control, the others actually entered an alliance with humans.

In that manner, humans’ place in the world was acknowledged. The end result was that humans... were the ones who unified Revered Ancient. Empress Summer Departure represented humankind. Ling’er represented the nonhumans. Starfire represented the gods. The three parties entered into a treaty agreement called Pure Ancient. The allied forces purged all the secret locations in the Revered Ancient mainland, and did everything possible to cleanse any outside influences.

Time passed. Another twenty years went by.

Xu Qing had now been in seclusion for forty years.

In the second set of twenty years, humankind’s position stabilized. Empress Summer Departure became Ancient Empress Summer Departure. Humankind advanced as well. The broken face was still there in the dome of heaven, leaving all living beings uneasy. Were it not for that, it would have been a golden age.

Ningyan grew up to be a remarkable individual. Due to the empress’ diligent guidance, he came to be exactly what one would expect of a crown prince. In addition to Ningyan, there were a few other people who grew into their own during those years.

For example, Wu Jianwu established his own set of core daoist teachings and doctrines. They focused on breeding animals. Though his cultivation base was not very high, through his partnership with the beasts that had been with him for so many years, he came to be extraordinary.

Then there was Kong Xianglong, who was a descendant of Palace Lord Kong Liangxiu of the Swordsage Palace in Sea-Sealing County. He continued to carry out the will of Kong Liangxiu, and eventually came to be the reigning palace lord. All he had to do was reach the appropriate level of cultivation base.

Everyone had their own path, and everyone achieved their own type of success.

It was the same with all the major forces in Revered Ancient. Humans, gods, and nonhumans maintained order. Slowly but surely, all connections to outside influence were identified, and records were kept about them. For all intents and purposes, there were no secret locations in Revered Ancient anymore.

With the exception... of one place! It was a place that no nonhuman, no god, and no human had ever entered by even half a step. Even Master Seventh only observed from the outside for a time before leaving it alone.

It was a very unique and special place in the Revered Ancient mainland. It was the Heaveneater Region! It was the place where the Sovereign Kingdom of Violet and Cyan had returned to!

No one entered the place, and no living thing from inside the Heaveneater Region ever left. Everybody seemed to be waiting.

***

Two years later... the dharmaboat that had been floating in the harbor in Seven Blood Eyes in South Phoenix for the past forty-two years quietly vanished into thin air. The only thing left behind were some ripples in the water.

The moment the dharmaboat vanished, someone materialized in Brilliant Heaven, right next to where Erniu was sleeping. Master Seventh, who sat cross-legged in front of his Master’s tomb, didn’t notice the new arrival.

The person who had arrived didn’t make any disturbance. He just looked at Erniu briefly, then disappeared.

A moment later, that same figure appeared in front of the statue of Grand Emperor Swordsage outside the imperial capital of humankind. No one saw him. No one even sensed him.

Xu Qing stood in front of the statue, looking up at Grand Emperor Swordsage. He wore a black robe and had long violet hair. He didn’t look any different than he had forty-two years ago. But there was something profound shimmering in his eyes. After looking at the statue for a long moment, he clasped hands and bowed.

Then he turned in the direction of Sea-Sealing County.

“She’s about to wake up...” he murmured. A warm smile appeared on his face as took a step in the direction of Sea-Sealing County.

***

In the complex deep beneath Sea-Sealing County was a phoenix palace. Within it was a lamp, slowly growing brighter. It was the Plumdark Evergreen Lamp.

The light of the lamp illuminated a woman seated cross-legged in the tranquil hall. She wore a gauzy, plum-colored gown that spread like clouds around her, drifting slowly as if caressed by a fragrant, invisible breeze. She was beautiful, with skin as fair as snow. Her brow seemed to hide infinite emotion, but at the same time, was the picture of elegant charm. She sat quietly on a rush cushion, her hands on her knees, her fingers long and slender.

From a distance, she looked as beautiful as a painting. It looked almost as if time had stopped in order to preserve her spectacular beauty for all time.

But then... a moment passed.

Her eyelashes fluttered, and she slowly opened her eyes and looked at the main door. Her eyes glittered like stars, vibrant enough to illuminate the whole world.

The door slowly opened.

The door of the phoenix palace slowly swung open. There was no wind outside, just flowing time that swept in as the door opened. As a result, it was as if the entire phoenix palace became a river of space-time. As the figure outside took a step, waves spread through the space-time.

When the first wave bloomed, the image within time spread through the interior hall. Within that image of shimmering ripples, it was possible to see the Seven Sect Coalition. Birdsong and the fragrance of flowers filled the air. Everything was harmonious.

Off in the distance was the new headquarters being constructed by Seven Blood Eyes cultivators. A bit closer beneath the dazzling starry sky was the Dark Serenity Sect, outside of which, two figures snuck along as stealthily as thieves. These were the days when Seven Blood Eyes had just joined the Seven Sect Coalition, turning it into the Eight Sect Coalition. At the moment Xu Qing had accepted Erniu’s invitation to join him in a business transaction with Huang Yikun, to sell a finger back to him.[1]

Up in the dome of heaven, a woman hovered, smiling. She was seductive, with long hair streaming down her back and bound loosely with a pink ribbon. Her violet garment was decorated with stars and glowed faintly. Surrounding her was a faint haze that made her truly seem like an immortal that didn’t belong in the mundane world.

Her gaze fell upon Xu Qing, and she laughed softly as she descended. To the astonishment of Erniu and Xu Qing both, she went right up to Xu Qing, put her finger under his chin, and exhaled softly.

“We meet again, child. What are you doing here at the Dark Serenity Sect so late at night? Are you lost?”

This was the first time that Xu Qing officially met Plumdark.

The waves undulated. Outside of the image in time, Xu Qing smiled. And then, the Xu Qing in the image looked up at the seductive woman and softly said, “I’m not lost. There’s an invisible string connected to my heart that I followed here.”

The words caused the woman to freeze in place.

The first wave in time sank down. On the outside, Xu Qing took a second step, and a second wave filled the hall.

The waves of the Everlasting Immortal Profundity River appeared, filling all that could be seen. It was evening, and the sun was setting. A large boat slowly sailed along the river.[2]

Plumdark sat on the rail looking at the glow of sunset. Xu Qing sat off to the side, looking cautious.

“Xu Qing,” she said quietly, “play that song again for me. I want to hear it.”

A pensive flute song drifted out. Though the song felt like something from the jianghu, it didn’t describe a life of sorrow, nor an existence of loneliness. The flute song swept out with a feeling of hope and joy.

Inside the image, Plumdark shivered and looked at Xu Qing.

As he sat there, he looked up and softly said, “This song used to be called Parting with Sorrow. Now it’s called Reunion.”
