Scenes like these filled the waves in the hall of the phoenix palace. As Xu Qing strode toward Plumdark, every step he took caused images within time to be replayed.

There was the time atop the statue of the huge snake, where they sat and had a heart-to-heart chat. There was the time in the private chamber in Sea-Sealing County when Plumdark put concealment symbols on him. There was the time in the imperial capital of humankind when Xu Qing snatched the Plumdark Evergreen Lamp. All of the images seemed to merge together, creating a trembling in space-time.[3]

Ultimately, Xu Qing strode through the waves until he stood right in front of the cross-legged Plumdark. He extended his hand toward her.

Her eyes glittered as if with starlight, which shone out to illuminate the world. And as Xu Qing approached, color entered that illuminated world. Without any hesitation, Plumdark took Xu Qing’s hand.

Xu Qing looked tenderly at her as she stood.

“I’m back,” he said softly. freewebnovel.com

After that, there was no sound in the phoenix palace. The complex beneath Sea-Sealing County blurred, and then everything disappeared.

When Xu Qing reappeared, he was no longer beneath Sea-Sealing County. Instead, he was atop Mount Daybreak, a place he had visited for years. There were now two gravestones there. This was the place Xu Qing had long since picked to be his home.[4]

His father and mother, who were already mere blurs in his memory, lay in rest here. They had been sacrificed to Eminent Desolation, so there was no way Xu Qing could find them in space-time. The only evidence of their existence came in the form of these two gravestones.

Together with Plumdark, Xu Qing settled down on Mount Daybreak. Half of a sixty-year-cycle passed.

During that time, civilization flourished in the Revered Ancient mainland. Zhou Zhengli and the others had already acclimated to life, and had gone their separate ways. Some had gone into seclusion, others had founded their own sects to expound their wisdom. After all, each had their own type of cultivation.

High in the dome of heaven, Eminent Desolation’s eyes never opened. However, two swords appeared on Mount Daybreak.

The first came twenty-seven years before, when a god from beyond Revered Ancient crossed the line of demarcation. The sword shot up from Mount Daybreak, into the dome of heaven, and out into the starry sky. There, it executed the god that had crossed the border. God blood fell. All living beings in Revered Ancient looked on.

The second sword came five years before. However, it didn’t fly to the starry sky, but rather, to the outer sea! In that location, a god from another star ring tried to use the Primeval Sea crossing method to reach Revered Ancient. That god was executed by the sword!

All gods observing from outside of Revered Ancient were shaken to the core by those swords.

Because of that, a true holy land actually came to exist in the mainland. People began to travel there, though few people actually stepped onto the mountain. The reason was that Mount Daybreak existed within space-time, but at the same time, didn’t exist.

There was one person who could step onto the mountain. However, when she arrived, she simply stood outside observing for a time, before finally deciding to leave. That person was Ling’er.

In life, there are some things that cannot be forced. And that is especially true of love. For example, despite a life of bitterness, Zhao Zhongheng had still not achieved the love he sought.

Decades ago when Xu Qing visited the Green Spirit Pharmacy, he had not stated anything openly. But in the days he had stayed, Ling’er had come to realize the truth.

Another ten years passed. One day as the sun set, the evening glow caused Mount Daybreak to shine radiantly.

A person appeared at the summit of the mountain. He wore a black robe and had long violet hair cascading down his shoulders. As he strode out, he seemed like a mysterious shimmer created by the afterglow of the setting sun. He was none other than Xu Qing.

Behind him was Plumdark, clad in garments that looked like those of a housewife. Her clothing was plain and simple, but she was as beautiful as ever. However, she looked worried, and seemed like she had something she wanted to say to Xu Qing. In the end, she maintained her silence.

Behind her, no longer in soul form, but in possession of a corporeal body, was Patriarch Golden Vajra Warrior. Over the past years, the patriarch had benefited from a lot of good fortune. He had become the steward of Mount Daybreak, and was able to throw his weight around anywhere he went outside the mountain. In his free time he had begun writing novels.... No one could challenge his authority except for Little Shadow....

However, the pride that usually imbued Patriarch Golden Vajra Warrior was gone. Instead, he looked just as worried as the lady of the house. He knew that now was not a time for him to speak. All he could do was step back silently and watch Xu Qing and Plumdark depart.

Plumdark paid no heed to the patriarch as she stepped in front of Xu Qing and adjusted his garments.

“You really have to go?” she asked.

Xu Qing didn’t say anything at first. A moment passed. He looked in the direction of the Heaveneater Region. “It’s time to end things. He’s been waiting for me for years now.”

The afterglow of the setting sun shone down on Mount Daybreak. For years, the mountain had experienced no daybreak. But for the past few decades, the sun shone dazzling on it. And right now, the afterglow made it more colorful than ever.

Two figures slowly parted. Outside the glowing light, Xu Qing strode farther and farther away. Inside the glowing light, Plumdark looked off into the distance.

Three days passed.

Xu Qing took his time going to the Heaveneater Region. As he walked, he looked around at the heaven and earth of Revered Ancient, and thought back to his youth. He thought about many things. He contemplated the things he had done, as well as the blurry images of his father and mother. He also thought about his older brother.

Three days later, beneath an evening glow similar to that on Mount Daybreak, he reached the northern border of the Heaveneater Region. The border itself was formed by a never-ending mountain range, pure black in color.

Xu Qing stood atop the mountain range, the wind buffeting his face as he looked out at what lay before him. On the other side of the mountains was a roiling black fog that covered everything and made it impossible to see the lands below. The fog covered all of the Heaveneater Region. Occasionally, shrill cries echoed out from it, as though an infinitude of demonic monsters roved about, casting a soul-chilling cold into the depths of anyone present.

A very strong mutagen filled the other side of the mountains, and thus the entirety of the Heaveneater Region. It was actually stronger than the mutagen Xu Qing had encountered in Brilliant Heaven. It seemed to be alive, and ready to devour any living thing it encountered.

To Xu Qing, it felt very similar to when the broken face’s eyes had opened over Peerless City or Supreme Ancient City.[1]

“This is a place where a godly aura has infected the mortal world, thus giving birth to countless grues.” The voice came from behind Xu Qing. Yu Liuchen stepped out of nothing to stand next to Xu Qing. Hē bowed. “Well met, Immortal Lord.”

Xu Qing turned to look at Yu Liuchen. He was not surprised. He had not concealed the fact that he was making this journey. What was more, he had long since come to understand more about Yu Liuchen.

Xu Qing shook his head. “I’m not an Immortal Lord.”

Yu Liuchen similarly shook hīs head. “You’re not an Immortal Lord, and yet, you surpass Immortal Lord. So what’s the difference?”

Xu Qing said nothing. He just looked back at the Heaveneater Region.

“Where gods are,” Yu Liuchen continued, “grues exist. Mortals don’t understand. Most cultivators don’t even understand. They think that grues and gods exist symbiotically. But many gods don’t believe that. In fact... Immortal Lords can also detect the same thing.... Grues do not exist symbiotically with gods. To a certain extent, you can say that they are a curse to gods!”

“You’re talking about the Grue World?” Xu Qing asked.[2]

Yu Liuchen’s eyes glittered with golden light. “Grues come before gods, and die because of gods. They turn into a curse, like a shadow that exists alongside the gods. That is why... gods above Altar God don’t....”

Upon reaching this point, Yu Liuchen shivered and stopped talking, as if having just been struck by some backlash. In fact, golden blood sprayed out of hīs mouth. “The natural laws of the higher star rings won’t allow me to explain. It would affect all higher living things. As for me, my special godly authority has allowed me to see some things that are normally kept secret....”

Yu Liuchen wiped the blood from hīs chin and looked at Xu Qing.

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed. Then he waved his right hand, causing a will of canon and statute to spread out. He looked at Yu Liuchen.

“Try again.”

Yu Liuchen took a moment to assess the surroundings, then took a deep breath, lowered hīs voice, and said, “Think hard. Of all the gods you’ve seen in your life that are above the Altar God level, isn’t it true that... none of thēm had shadows??”

Yu Liuchen’s words caused Xu Qing’s eyes to glitter.

“Shadows are mediums of the Grue World,” Yu Liuchen continued. “At the same time, they are curses to the gods. This knowledge has been tampered with by the higher natural laws, ensuring that no living beings notice the truth.”

As Yu Liuchen continued to speak, hē trembled and began to sweat profusely.

Xu Qing thought about it, and realized that it was true. None of the gods above the Altar God level that he had ever encountered had shadows. He had just never noticed it before.

“How interesting...” Xu Qing said calmly. “So you came here to explain more about this?”

Yu Liuchen looked at Xu Qing and bowed deeply. “I guessed that you would come to the Heaveneater Region, Immortal Lord. I’ve been waiting here for decades, during which time I’ve targeted the area by telling a total of 370,000 stories.

“Without exception, every single one of those stories ended up being switched with the will of a grue. As a result, I was not able to finish any of the stories. I believe it has something to do with the Grue World. Immortal Lord, that brother of yours... I suspect there’s something about his identity that isn’t so hidden....”

Xu Qing looked at Yu Liuchen and nodded.

Yu Liuchen let loose a sigh. Hē had come here in order to tell Xu Qing these things. Now, hē didn’t want to stay any longer. Stepping back, hē disappeared into thin air, leaving behind only some encouraging words for Xu Qing. “I truly hope things go smoothly for you, and that you achieve that which you desire.” freewebnovel.com

The wind seemed to blow a bit stronger on the mountaintop.

“Achieve that which I desire...” Xu Qing murmured. A few breaths of time passed, and then he stepped into the black fog of the Heaveneater Region.

Inside the border of the Heaveneater Region was... the Sovereign Kingdom of Violet and Cyan! At that moment, the entire place trembled. The boundless black fog that filled the Heaveneater Region began to churn, and it quickly turned into a raging sea. Within every furious wave on that sea were ear-piercing screaming sounds. The sound was an intense force of expulsion that sought to eject Xu Qing! Numerous sinister auras swept through the black fog, filled with malice and intense madness as they converged on him.

Face completely expressionless, Xu Qing lifted his right foot and stepped down. A sound like millions upon millions of thunderclaps exploded out. At the same time, a special destiny aura swirled around Xu Qing, turning into an imperial crown that settled onto his head. Intangible pressure radiated out in all directions.

The special destiny aura... had the same origin as the Sovereign Kingdom of Violet and Cyan! Where it passed, the fog was sent spinning off to the side, revealing a desolate and barren world. The countless streams of malicious will that existed in the fog lurched to a halt, then melted. The environment was no longer cold and sinister. What was more, the force of expulsion reversed, and became a joyous, welcoming cheer!

The reason was that half of the special destiny aura that formed the imperial crown was actually the destiny aura of the Sovereign Kingdom of Violet and Cyan!

Years ago, the Crown Prince of Violet and Cyan had carried out a complex scheme that had not fully succeeded, as Master Seventh resurrected Xu Qing, and Xu Qing had taken half of the destiny aura! Now, that missing half had returned. A half-emperor had returned.[3]

The Sovereign Kingdom of Violet and Cyan, which had come back from antiquity to devour the Heaveneater Region, began to tremble. The black fog roiled more violently than it had all those years ago.

As the kingdom shook, Xu Qing took a second step forward. That step spanned a great distance. When he reappeared... he was in the capital city of the Sovereign Kingdom of Violet and Cyan.

He saw the city itself, and all the citizens that the black fog had concealed. The city looked like a series of ink paintings, blurry, yet clearly defined by an ancient style. The citizens... were the same. They looked like they had been painted into the scene. Amidst the numerous buildings were men, women, elderly, and young ones. It didn’t matter their status or identity, they all looked the same.

When Xu Qing appeared, it was as if drops of color had spilled onto the painting. The painting instantly became brighter, and at the same time, all the citizens noticed what was happening. Their gazes were full of hatred, madness, and confusion. It seemed like they wanted to pounce on Xu Qing, but he was blessed by the destiny aura of the kingdom. As dead spirits that existed only because of destiny aura, they had no choice but to bow their heads.

Xu Qing saw all of this. Then he focused his attention on the palace. He took a third step. When that step landed, he appeared in the very center of the capital city... at Zi Qing’s imperial palace!

He stood in a black square in front of the main hall. Visible in front of him was an enormous, holy statue. It was... the only statue of the broken face of Eminent Desolation! The statue was clearly a lifeless thing. But it emanated an intense pressure that ensured the entire imperial palace was absolutely silent.

Behind the statue was the open door leading into the hall. Inside the hall, a person sat on the Dragon Throne!

He wore an imperial crown, imperial robes, had violet hair, and was extremely attractive, albeit somewhat sinister. He was none other than... Zi Qing, the Crown Prince of Violet and Cyan! His head leaned against one hand as he looked at Xu Qing outside. A warm smile appeared on his charming, nefarious face.

When he spoke, it was in a warm voice that cut through the gruish, stifling atmosphere. “Just what I would expect of my lil’ bro. You’re clearly as clever as when you were young. You didn’t come to face me in your immortal-god fusion state. In fact, you didn’t even bring your god clone into my kingdom. However, that doesn’t matter. What matters, lil’ bro, is that you’re finally here.”

Inside of the imperial palace of the Sovereign Kingdom of Violet and Cyan, Zi Qing sat on the Dragon Throne. Outside, Xu Qing stood in the square. Their gazes locked.

Xu Qing remembered that the last time they had exchanged a glance was when he had died outside of the imperial capital of humankind.

The time before that was in the rain in Emperor-Receiving Prefecture. At that earlier time, Zi Qing had just killed Master Sixth.[1]

Those images were currently flashing through Xu Qing’s mind. However, compared to those previous instances... this time, Xu Qing’s gaze was very calm.

He looked at the Crown Prince of Violet and Cyan. Given their proximity, he could tell that Zi Qing was only an Altar God. Years ago in the imperial capital of humankind, Zi Qing had used Empress Summer Departure’s breakthrough to carry out his own ceremony and step into the Altar God level. From the look of it, even after all the years that had passed, he had not progressed past that point. He was still an Altar God.[2]

However, Xu Qing would not be careless because of that. He knew... that with the statue of the broken face of Eminent Desolation present, cultivation levels didn’t really matter.

Zi Qing was a clever schemer, and would have many contingency plans in place.

Facing Zi Qing, Xu Qing coolly said, “It doesn’t matter if I fuse with my god clone or not. If I brought it into your presence, then... Considering it was made from the flesh and blood of Eminent Desolation, it’s hard to say if it would continue to belong to me.”

Zi Qing smiled warmly. “Very clever, lil’ bro. I can see that you’ve prepared well.”

The Crown Prince of Violet and Cyan lifted his right hand toward the sky and made a beckoning gesture. The canopy of heaven rumbled as a huge vortex appeared. All of the black fog was swept into it. And then an image formed in the middle of the vortex.

Within the image was... Mount Daybreak! It was clearly visible. And thus, it was easy to see that, seated cross-legged inside Mount Daybreak, was a figure that pulsed with a godly aura. It was none other than Xu Qing’s god clone!

The clone was surrounded by a complex spell formation, which was active, and filled the area with a terrifying power of suppression. Beyond the spell formation, and outside of Mount Daybreak, were several people. They were Zhou Zhengli, Sir Star Ring, and the others. All were seated cross-legged and performing incantation gestures, which sent power out to bolster the spell formation in Mount Daybreak. As a result, the power of suppression was augmented.

However, none of that was very important. The primary force suppressing Xu Qing’s god clone... was Master Seventh! He sat cross-legged at the summit of Mount Daybreak, his full strength focused on the god clone.

Everything seemed to be going normally. But then Zi Qing made that beckoning gesture, and the god clone shivered within the midst of the spell formation. Then the clone’s eyes opened! Golden light spilled out... as well as something vile and nefarious. It was as if the clone was not Xu Qing!

Terrifying power surged out of the clone, clearly seeking to destroy the spell formation and smash through the mountain toward the source of the beckoning gesture. As soon as that power hit the spell formation, it began to decay and crumble. Zhou Zhengli and the others trembled violently as they did everything possible to bolster the formation. Blood sprayed out of Zhou Zhengli’s mouth. The same happened to Sir Star Ring. Sir Vilespirit, Li Mengtu, Yuanshan Su, and all the others felt their minds reeling as blood oozed out of their eyes, ears, noses, and mouths.

Even as it seemed impossible to maintain control, Master Seventh snorted coldly and pushed his right hand down onto the mountain. That gesture caused the power of Deep Earth to pour forth, isolating the mountain! Then he lifted his left hand, revealing an item within it. It was a mirror shard! It was the very same gift Immortal Lord Mi Ming had given to Xu Qing, and it contained the might of his canon and statute.

In combination with Master Seventh’s Deep Earth power, it could isolate Mount Daybreak and ensure that the god clone... had no way of breaking free. Although it would only work temporarily, it was at least enough to block Zi Qing’s first summons.

This was one of the preemptive measures Xu Qing had taken before coming to the Sovereign Kingdom of Violet and Cyan.

He had long since come to a realization. There was a deep connection between Zi Qing and Eminent Desolation. Therefore, a clone that had been made from the flesh and blood of Eminent Desolation... would definitely reveal flaws in the presence of Zi Qing! Xu Qing had been well aware that he needed to suppress the god clone before coming to the Sovereign Kingdom of Violet and Cyan, just to make sure nothing unexpected happened.

At the same time, without his god clone, he couldn’t enter his immortal-god fusion state, which was the strongest state he could achieve. Instead, he would have to rely only on his immortal body.

That was one of the reasons he had gone into seclusion! He had hoped to achieve a breakthrough! Unfortunately, the decades in seclusion had not been enough to become an Immortal Lord, not even after fully absorbing the light that had been worshiped by the Brilliant Heaven Godfolk! His canon and statute was sufficient, but rising from Summer Immortal to Immortal Lord just required too much ringsource.

After decades absorbing the mysterious light worshiped by the Brilliant Heaven Godfolk, it finally ran out. The light had ringsource, but it wasn’t enough for Xu Qing. And what he didn’t take was the part of the light that served as a key. It could not be taken away by an outside force. That was why Xu Qing had left seclusion and come to the Sovereign Kingdom of Violet and Cyan.

The image of Mount Daybreak within the vortex wavered. Down in the square, Xu Qing looked up. Eyes glowing brightly, he waved his hand toward the sky. The vortex above surged, then trembled as it started spinning faster and faster in the opposite direction.

At the same time, Xu Qing’s cultivation base began to rise. The fluctuations of late Summer Immortal spread through heaven and earth, filling the Heaveneater Region, and turning into an external force that controlled the vortex.

Xu Qing looked at Zi Qing and spoke in a booming dao voice. “Seize!”

His voice marked the beginning of a grand ceremony in the imperial capital of humankind. All of the powerful human experts had gathered for the ceremony, which called on destiny aura and heeded the commands of Empress Summer Departure. As the ceremony activated, intense light rose up from the imperial capital and shot toward... the Heaveneater Region.

Upon sensing the human ceremony beginning, the species in all the other major regions in Revered Ancient began ceremonies that they had prepared. All of them called on the full power of their species.

Streams of light shot high, then screamed in the direction of Xu Qing in the Heaveneater Region. These things take time to describe, but in reality, happened in an instant. Beams of light from countless species joined that from humankind to pierce through the air, becoming like shooting stars that appeared over the Heaveneater Region.

There, they became one. The heavenly daos of Revered Ancient were manifest in the light. Emperor Ancient Spirit was there, as was Xu Qing’s heavenly dao son.

When all of that light combined, it turned into... a huge mirror hanging over the Heaveneater Region. The surface of the mirror reflected all of the lands of the Heaveneater Region, including every mountain and river! It also reflected the imperial palace! As the mirror reflected the Heaveneater Region, and as the vortex spun in reverse, blurring, streams of destiny aura materialized, becoming streams of gray energy that were pulled into the mirror!

As a result, the blurry image of the region in the mirror quickly began to turn clear! This was a case of... heavenly daos seizing the destiny aura of a kingdom!

Xu Qing had converged the power of countless species to form the Mirror of Revered Ancient, which hovered above the Heaveneater Region and took its destiny aura.

This was only one part of Xu Qing’s plan. The Crown Prince of Violet and Cyan wanted to seize his god clone. So he chose to use his half of the destiny aura of the Sovereign Kingdom of Violet and Cyan to seize the other half of the destiny aura.

Inside the imperial palace, atop the Dragon Throne, Zi Qing looked at what was happening, and his smile broadened. He gave Xu Qing a slight nod.

“How amusing. You’ve grown up, lil’ bro. You even understand that you should steal the family fortune from your big brother. Except, do you know how much of the family fortune there is?”

Zi Qing smiled.

Fate!

When he spoke, the giant book formed from the lands of the Heaveneater Region began flipping through pages more quickly. And now, the Mirror of Revered Ancient didn’t have time to blur the contents and absorb all the destiny aura. Every single page was the Sovereign Kingdom of Violet and Cyan!

Yet in the moment of failure, as Xu Qing stood in the square outside the grand hall, his eyes turned cold, and he burst into motion. Inside the hall, Zi Qing gently flicked his finger. A ripple of fate flowed out from his fingertip, which blocked Xu Qing from entering.

“Your opponent will be another possible version of me, extracted from fate.”

As the words left his mouth, the pages suddenly stopped flipping. As a result, one subsidiary branch of fate became prominent. When that branch appeared, it subverted reality. Or perhaps it was most correct to say that it appeared at the same time, right there in the hall!

The Crown Prince of Violet and Cyan still sat on the Dragon Throne in the hall. But outside the hall, dramatic things were happening!

A second Zi Qing had appeared in the square! He stood atop the statue of Eminent Desolation’s broken face. His arms were stretched wide, and his expression was evil and cold. And he had just completed saying something that he had begun to speak while in the subsidiary branch of fate.

“... sacrifice!”

As that final word echoed out, countless fanatical responses came from within the Sovereign Kingdom of Violet and Cyan in that branch of fate.

“I’m willing to meet death for the sake of the crown prince!”

“I’m willing to meet death for the sake of the crown prince!!”

All citizens of the kingdom from that branch of fate shouted the same thing, including cultivators, mortals, men, women, young ones, and the elderly. There were no exceptions, and their faces were completely fanatical.

And in response to Zi Qing’s words, all of them burst into flames... to sacrifice themselves! They were sacrificing themselves... to the Crown Prince of Violet and Cyan! And then, the Zi Qing from that branch of fate took the sacrifice of the entire kingdom and absorbed it into himself! Countless streams of sacrificed life force shot toward the statue of Eminent Desolation’s broken face, where they merged into Zi Qing. There seemed no end to them.

Xu Qing did nothing to stop them. Doing so would have been pointless. With his canon and statute, he could sense that what was happening had already occurred in the past. Trying to change it would have been impossible.

But if he waited until the act was complete, he could reverse the karma. Therefore, he paid very close attention to every detail of what was happening.

As Zi Qing atop the statue of Eminent Desolation rapidly absorbed all the sacrifices, his body began to melt into drops of blood that fell onto the statue. The process only took a few breaths of time....

Xu Qing watched as all of the citizens in the branch of fate disappeared. What was more, that version of Zi Qing melted, and his blood... eventually covered the statue and everything surrounding it. Then, a terrifying aura erupted from the statue, which shot up and turned into a majestic godly might!

Heaven and earth flashed with wild colors. Winds screamed in every direction. Mutagen filled the world. Natural laws actually disappeared, and magical laws ceased to exist. This godly authority became the only thing that existed! This was the majesty of the God Lord level!

Because of that majesty, the statue of Eminent Desolation transformed, as if waking up. It turned into a body of flesh and blood! The flesh and blood wriggled and began changing appearance. It became humanoid in shape! In the blink of an eye, the facial features... became an exact copy of Zi Qing!

The figure took a single step and vanished. Upon reappearing, hē was right in front of Xu Qing, pulsing with mutagen and the pressure of a God Lord. Reaching out, hē pushed hīs hand in the direction of Xu Qing.

Xu Qing’s canon and statute collapsed due to Zi Qing’s touch. Rumbling sounds filled heaven and earth! The entire world trembled as a massive attack hit Xu Qing. He was shoved backward, stopping after only about 300 meters. There, he looked calmly at Zi Qing standing outside the hall.

That version of Zi Qing was looking back at him. Behind hīm was the other Zi Qing, also looking at Xu Qing.
